<p><b><a href="/wiki/September" title="September">September</a></b> <b><a href="/wiki/2008" title="2008">2008</a></b> was the ninth month of that leap year. The month, which began on a <a href="/wiki/Monday" title="Monday">Monday</a>, ended on a <a href="/wiki/Tuesday" title="Tuesday">Tuesday</a> after 30 days.</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portal:Current_events"><a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Portal:Current events</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/September_2008&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Portal:Current events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i>This is an <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events/How_to_archive_the_portal" title="Portal:Current events/How to archive the portal">archived version</a> of Wikipedia's <a href="/wiki/Portal:Current_events" title="Portal:Current events">Current events Portal</a> from September 2008.</i></p>

<table cellspacing="0" class="plainlinks" style="background-color:#cef2e0" width="100%">
<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 1, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-01</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_1&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_1&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_1&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S." title="U.S.">U.S.</a> <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> <a href="/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_United_States" title="Vice President of the United States">Vice Presidential</a> candidate <a href="/wiki/Sarah_Palin" title="Sarah Palin">Sarah Palin</a>'s 17-year-old daughter <a href="/wiki/Bristol_Palin" title="Bristol Palin">Bristol</a> is revealed to be five months pregnant. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/7592636.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/newstopics/uselection2008/johnmccain/2662794/John-McCains-running-mate-Sarah-Palins-teenage-daughter-is-pregnant.html" rel="nofollow">(Telegraph.co.uk)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5jIMJWupyWNmvU3UX2aGhICmZrQ_wD92U1M600" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/americas/2008/09/200891172722676472.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.wsj.com/washwire/2008/09/01/mccain-camp-offers-talking-points-on-palin-pregnancy/" rel="nofollow">(Wall Street Journal)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_of_the_United_States" title="Military of the United States">U.S. military</a> hands control of <a href="/wiki/Al_Anbar_Governorate" title="Al Anbar Governorate">Al Anbar Governorate</a> over to the <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> government. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/7591111.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>An <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ACLU" title="ACLU">ACLU</a> lawsuit challenges <a href="/wiki/Gag_order" title="Gag order">gag orders</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/National_Security_Letter" title="National Security Letter">National Security Letters</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://arstechnica.com/newsap.google.com/article/ALeqM5hblwpbfkh_9JH9nsNU1Xn9ttNKKQD92U0EA00" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/7591197.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2008 Atlantic hurricane season">2008 Atlantic hurricane season</a>:
<ul>
<li>Tropical Storm Hanna becomes <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hanna_(2008)" title="Hurricane Hanna (2008)">Hurricane Hanna (2008)</a> with hurricane warnings issued for the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bahamas" title="Bahamas">Bahamas</a> and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos" title="Turks and Caicos">Turks and Caicos</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/26496933/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Ike_(2008)" title="Tropical Storm Ike (2008)">Tropical Storm Ike (2008)</a> forms east of the <a href="/wiki/Leeward_Islands" title="Leeward Islands">Leeward Islands</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.miamiherald.com/news/broward/breaking-news/story/667427.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Miami Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gustav_(2008)" title="Hurricane Gustav (2008)">Hurricane Gustav</a> weakens to a tropical storm in central <a href="/wiki/Louisiana" title="Louisiana">Louisiana</a> after being responsible for 7 deaths in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> and more than 90 in the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">Caribbean</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/2008/09/01/Gustav_weakens_to_tropical_storm/UPI-30601220263816/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_South_Ossetia_war" title="2008 South Ossetia war">2008 South Ossetia war</a>:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> suspends talks on a new partnership agreement with <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> until Russian troops have withdrawn from <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/7592541.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> accuses the West of sending weapons to <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> along with aid, while the <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a> considers possible <a href="/wiki/Economic_sanctions" title="Economic sanctions">sanctions</a> against Russia. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/europe/09/01/russia.georgia.summit.sanctions/index.html?section=cnn_latest" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Yasuo_Fukuda" title="Yasuo Fukuda">Yasuo Fukuda</a> abruptly resigns less than a year after taking office, triggering a <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democratic_Party_(Japan)_leadership_election,_2008" title="Liberal Democratic Party (Japan) leadership election, 2008">leadership election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/7591969.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Orissa" title="Government of Orissa">Government of Orissa</a> report states 558 <a href="/wiki/House" title="House">houses</a> and 17 places of worship were burnt in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Orissa_violence" title="2008 Orissa violence">2008 Orissa violence</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/India/558_houses_17_places_of_worship_torched_during_riot_Orissa_govt/rssarticleshow/3431842.cms" rel="nofollow">(Times of India)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Robert_French" title="Robert French">Robert French</a> is sworn in as the 12th <a href="/wiki/Chief_Justice_of_Australia" title="Chief Justice of Australia">Chief Justice of Australia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2008/09/01/2351772.htm?section=australia" rel="nofollow">(ABC (Australia))</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City Football Club</a> is bought out by the <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Abu_Dhabi_United_Group_for_Investment_and_Development_Limited&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Abu Dhabi United Group for Investment and Development Limited (page does not exist)">Abu Dhabi United Group for Investment and Development Limited</a>, the consortium led by <a href="/wiki/Mansour_bin_Zayed_Al_Nahyan" title="Mansour bin Zayed Al Nahyan">Sheikh Mansour bin Zayed Al Nahyan</a>. This effectively made City the richest Football Club in the world. It also made <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Transfer_Deadline_Day&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Transfer Deadline Day (page does not exist)">Transfer Deadline Day</a> one of the most memorable, with City's new found wealth allowing them to bid for such players as <a href="/wiki/Dimitar_Berbatov" title="Dimitar Berbatov">Dimitar Berbatov</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Torres" title="Fernando Torres">Fernando Torres</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mario_Gomez" title="Mario Gomez">Mario Gomez</a> and <a href="/wiki/David_Villa" title="David Villa">David Villa</a>. They eventually signed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Robson_de_Souza" title="Robson de Souza">Robinho</a> for a British Record Fee of £32.5million. The takeover and the Robinho deal as a whole sent shockwaves throughout the Sporting world. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/sport/football/premier-league/manchester-city-takeover-complete-914841.html" rel="nofollow">(Independent)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 2, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-02</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_2&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_2&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_2&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>New study shows that children of older fathers are at higher risk of psychological conditions such as <a href="/wiki/Bipolar_disorder" title="Bipolar disorder">bipolar disorder</a>, <a href="/wiki/Autism" title="Autism">autism</a> and <a href="/wiki/Schizophrenia" title="Schizophrenia">schizophrenia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/newsOne/idUSL138021820080901" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>A gunman goes on a <a href="/wiki/Spree_killer" title="Spree killer">shooting spree</a> that leaves 6 people, including a police deputy, dead, and four injured, in <a href="/wiki/Alger,_Washington" title="Alger, Washington">Alger, Washington</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>.<a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/stories/2008/09/02/national/main4409150.shtml" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/United_States_Environmental_Protection_Agency" title="United States Environmental Protection Agency">Environmental Protection Agency</a> vetoes plans by the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army_Corps_of_Engineers" title="United States Army Corps of Engineers">Army Corps of Engineers</a> to build the world's largest water pump on the <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_River" title="Mississippi River">Mississippi River</a> <a href="/wiki/Mississippi_River_Delta" title="Mississippi River Delta">Delta</a> raising concerns about the impact on wetlands. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/nation/27770314.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Minneapolis StarTribune</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2008 Atlantic hurricane season">2008 Atlantic hurricane season</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gustav_(2008)" title="Hurricane Gustav (2008)">Hurricane Gustav</a> weakens to a tropical depression. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/news/world/gustav-wind-runs-out-of-puff/2008/09/02/1220121234689.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> adopts a platform at its <a href="/wiki/2008_Republican_National_Convention" title="2008 Republican National Convention">national convention</a> that is critical of <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_McCain" title="John McCain">John McCain</a> for their support of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Too_Big_to_Fail_policy" title="Too Big to Fail policy">government bailouts of companies</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601087&amp;sid=aMdtdOg3_lBY&amp;refer=home" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Thai_political_crisis" title="2008 Thai political crisis">2008 Thai political crisis</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> <a href="/wiki/List_of_Prime_Ministers_of_Thailand" title="List of Prime Ministers of Thailand">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Samak_Sundaravej" title="Samak Sundaravej">Samak Sundaravej</a> declares a <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">state of emergency</a> in <a href="/wiki/Bangkok" title="Bangkok">Bangkok</a> after clashes between groups of pro- and <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Alliance_for_Democracy" title="People's Alliance for Democracy">anti-government</a> protesters resulted in one death and 43 injuries. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/7592942.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Anupong Paochinda, the Commander-in-Chief of the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Thai_Army" title="Royal Thai Army">Royal Thai Army</a>, states that the Army "will not use force" in enforcing the state of emergency. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5hG71oGl1LokvZphtDQZzL44nzc3QD92UEG3O0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A memorial service is held for the 229 victims of <a href="/wiki/Swissair_Flight_111" title="Swissair Flight 111">Swissair Flight 111</a>, with some present complaining about a perceived lack of action by the authorities to prevent future disasters. <a class="external text" href="http://canadianpress.google.com/article/ALeqM5gW9-VI7ohlmDGaZL1wbx8xNw271w" rel="nofollow">(Canadian Press)</a> <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikinews.org/wiki/Service_held_in_Nova_Scotia_on_tenth_anniversary_of_Swissair_crash_that_killed_229" title="n:Service held in Nova Scotia on tenth anniversary of Swissair crash that killed 229">(Wikinews)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 3, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-03</span>)</span> (Wednesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_3&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_3&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_3&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> officially endorses <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">Arizona</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_of_the_United_States" title="Senate of the United States">Senator</a> <a href="/wiki/John_McCain" title="John McCain">John McCain</a> as its candidate in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_United_States_presidential_election" title="2008 United States presidential election">2008 United States presidential election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/04/us/politics/04repubday.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2008 Atlantic hurricane season">2008 Atlantic hurricane season</a>:
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike_(2008)" title="Hurricane Ike (2008)">Hurricane Ike</a> becomes the fifth <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane" title="Hurricane">hurricane</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2008_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2008 Atlantic hurricane season">2008 Atlantic hurricane season</a>, later strengthening to Category 3. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/weather/storms/hurricanes/2008-09-03-hurricane-ike_N.htm?csp=34" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5gVWjsPEiqe1tEu2mhBIRaxxGi8owD92VIBMG0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>Flooding from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Hanna_(2008)" title="Tropical Storm Hanna (2008)">Tropical Storm Hanna</a> causes 26 deaths in <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5gVWjsPEiqe1tEu2mhBIRaxxGi8owD92VIBMG0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_Army" title="United States Army">United States Army</a> troops cross the <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> border and launch a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Angoor_Ada_raid" title="Angoor Ada raid">raid in the Angoor Ada region</a> of <a href="/wiki/Waziristan" title="Waziristan">Waziristan</a>. Twenty civilians die. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/story?id=5718172&amp;page=1" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a>
<ul>
<li>Earlier 'up to 90' people were killed during US <a href="/wiki/Airstrike" title="Airstrike">air raid</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Herat_province" title="Herat province">Herat province</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Afganistan" title="Afganistan">Afganistan</a>, many of them women and children, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Afganistan" title="Afganistan">Afgan</a> government and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UN" title="UN">UN</a> said. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/HRW" title="HRW">HRW</a> says <a href="/wiki/Civilian" title="Civilian">civilians</a> deaths from international air strikes nearly tripled between 2006 and 2007. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/7603969.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/GMAC_ResCap" title="GMAC ResCap">GMAC</a>'s Residential Capital mortgage provider announces plans to dramatically reduce the size of its business resulting in the loss of 5,000 jobs. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/business/27813299.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Minneapolis-St Paul Star-Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kyodo" title="Kyodo">Kyodo</a> news agency reports that <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> has started rebuilding the <a href="/wiki/Yongbyon_Nuclear_Scientific_Research_Center" title="Yongbyon Nuclear Scientific Research Center">Yongbyon Nuclear Scientific Research Center</a> in retaliation for the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> failing to remove it from a list of states that sponsor <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorism</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/asiapcf/09/03/north.korea.nuclear/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Court_of_Appeals_for_the_Eighth_Circuit" title="United States Court of Appeals for the Eighth Circuit">United States Court of Appeals for the Eighth Circuit</a> finds "that a reliance on information in <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> is insufficient grounds for a ruling" in an immigration case. <a class="external text" href="http://arstechnica.com/news.ars/post/20080902-appeals-court-smacks-down-judge-for-relying-on-wikipedia.html" rel="nofollow">(Ars Technica)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Pakistan" title="Prime Minister of Pakistan">Prime Minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yousaf_Raza_Gilani" title="Yousaf Raza Gilani">Yousaf Raza Gilani</a> survives an assassination attempt. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/south_asia/7595572.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Independent_Monitoring_Commission" title="Independent Monitoring Commission">Independent Monitoring Commission</a> reports that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Provisional_IRA" title="Provisional IRA">Provisional IRA</a> has effectively been disbanded as a terrorist organization, but the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Provisional_IRA_Army_Council" title="Provisional IRA Army Council">Provisional IRA Army Council</a> still exists. <a class="external text" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/uk/2008/sep/03/northernireland.ireland?gusrc=rss&amp;feed=networkfront" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Guardian</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_of_the_United_States" title="Senate of the United States">Senator</a> <a href="/wiki/John_McCain" title="John McCain">John McCain</a> officially accepts the nomination of the <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2008" title="United States presidential election, 2008">United States presidential election, 2008</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/05/us/politics/05repubs.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Former <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> political <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lobbyist" title="Lobbyist">lobbyist</a> <a href="/wiki/Jack_Abramoff" title="Jack Abramoff">Jack Abramoff</a> is sentenced to four years in prison for his role in the <a href="/wiki/Jack_Abramoff_scandals" title="Jack Abramoff scandals">Jack Abramoff scandals</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://cbs13.com/national/jack.abramoff.prison.2.810348.html" rel="nofollow">(CBS)</a></li>
<li>The death toll from <a href="/wiki/Flood" title="Flood">flooding</a> in <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haiti</a> caused by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Hanna_(2008)" title="Tropical Storm Hanna (2008)">Tropical Storm Hanna</a> rises to 61. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/US/weather/09/04/hurricanes.hanna.ike/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Thailand" title="Government of Thailand">Government of Thailand</a> agrees to hold a <a href="/wiki/Thai_vote_of_confidence_referendum,_2008" title="Thai vote of confidence referendum, 2008">referendum</a> to resolve the <a href="/wiki/2008_Thai_political_crisis" title="2008 Thai political crisis">2008 Thai political crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5hG71oGl1LokvZphtDQZzL44nzc3QD92VO3U82" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tata_Motors" title="Tata Motors">Tata Motors</a> suspends work at its <a href="/wiki/Tata_Nano" title="Tata Nano">Tata Nano</a> plant at <a href="/wiki/Singur" title="Singur">Singur</a>, <a href="/wiki/West_Bengal" title="West Bengal">West Bengal</a>, due to continued agitations from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Trinamul_Congress" title="Trinamul Congress">Trinamul Congress</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thehindu.com/2008/09/03/stories/2008090358390100.htm" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Hindu</i>)</a></li>
<li>Physicists at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fermi_National_Accelerator_Laboratory" title="Fermi National Accelerator Laboratory">Fermi National Accelerator Laboratory</a> report the discovery of the <a href="/wiki/Omega_baryon" title="Omega baryon"><span style="white-space:nowrap;"><span style="display:inline-block;margin-bottom:-0.3em;vertical-align:0.8em;line-height:1.0em;font-size:80%;text-align:right"><br/></span>Ω<span style="display:inline-block;margin-bottom:-0.3em;vertical-align:-0.4em;line-height:1.0em;font-size:80%;text-align:left">−<br/>
b</span></span></a>, a "doubly-<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Strangeness_(particle_physics)" title="Strangeness (particle physics)">strange</a>" <a href="/wiki/Baryon" title="Baryon">baryon</a> containing two <a href="/wiki/Strange_quark" title="Strange quark">strange quarks</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Bottom_quark" title="Bottom quark">bottom quark</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sciencedaily.com/releases/2008/09/080903172201.htm" rel="nofollow">(Science Daily)</a></li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_5&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>Five hundred people have died in the <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haitian</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Gona%C3%AFves" title="Gonaïves">Gonaïves</a> as a result of flooding caused by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Hanna_(2008)" title="Tropical Storm Hanna (2008)">Tropical Storm Hanna</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/story/0,10117,24303444-401,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via News Limited)</a></li>
<li>According to several news reports, the US government plans to take control of <a href="/wiki/Fannie_Mae" title="Fannie Mae">Fannie Mae</a> and <a href="/wiki/Freddie_Mac" title="Freddie Mac">Freddie Mac</a> in a takeover plan. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/26567533/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>Estimates of sea-level rise due to <a href="/wiki/Global_warming" title="Global warming">global warming</a> are scaled back. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/scienceNews/idUSN0442173820080904?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=scienceNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Condoleezza_Rice" title="Condoleezza Rice">Condoleezza Rice</a> becomes the first <a href="/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State" title="United States Secretary of State">United States Secretary of State</a> to visit <a href="/wiki/Libya" title="Libya">Libya</a> since <a href="/wiki/1953" title="1953">1953</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nydailynews.com/news/us_world/2008/09/05/2008-09-05_sect_of_state_condoleezza_rice_arrives_i.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via the <i>New York Daily News</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> reinstates <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Pakistan" title="Supreme Court of Pakistan">Supreme Court</a> judges ousted by former <a href="/wiki/President_of_Pakistan" title="President of Pakistan">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Pervez_Musharraf" title="Pervez Musharraf">Pervez Musharraf</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/asiapcf/09/05/pakistan.judges/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Unemployment" title="Unemployment">unemployment</a> rate in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> rises to its highest level since <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/December_2003" title="December 2003">December 2003</a> after the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/US_economy" title="US economy">US economy</a> loses 84,000 jobs in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/August_2008" title="August 2008">August 2008</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/business/7600379.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/La_Princesse" title="La Princesse">La Princesse</a>, a giant mechanical spider, starts to roam the streets of <a href="/wiki/Liverpool" title="Liverpool">Liverpool</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>, as part of the 2008 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/European_City_of_Culture" title="European City of Culture">European City of Culture</a> celebrations. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/england/merseyside/7599960.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">European Union</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/Rosetta_(spacecraft)" title="Rosetta (spacecraft)">Rosetta</a></i> spacecraft performs a flyby of the <a href="/wiki/Asteroid" title="Asteroid">asteroid</a> <a href="/wiki/2867_%C5%A0teins" title="2867 Šteins">2867 Šteins</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.afp.com/english/news/stories/newsmlmmd.97b8498abdf4c4bb14d2896245c9323d.341.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Quentin_Bryce" title="Quentin Bryce">Quentin Bryce</a> is sworn in as the first female <a href="/wiki/Governor-General_of_Australia" title="Governor-General of Australia">Governor-General of Australia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.theage.com.au/national/bryce-sworn-in-as-governorgeneral-20080905-4a21.html" rel="nofollow">(AAP via <i>The Melbourne Age</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Morris_Iemma" title="Morris Iemma">Morris Iemma</a> resigns as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Premiers_of_New_South_Wales" title="Premiers of New South Wales">Premier</a> of <a href="/wiki/New_South_Wales" title="New South Wales">New South Wales</a> following a loss of support in the <a href="/wiki/Australian_Labor_Party" title="Australian Labor Party">Australian Labor Party</a> <a href="/wiki/Caucus" title="Caucus">caucus</a>, and is replaced by <a href="/wiki/Nathan_Rees" title="Nathan Rees">Nathan Rees</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.smh.com.au/news/national/nathan-rees-confirmed-as-new-nsw-premier/2008/09/05/1220121494217.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Pacific_hurricane_season" title="2008 Pacific hurricane season">2008 Pacific hurricane season</a>: Tropical Storm Lowell forms off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/disp/story.mpl/front/5987712.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Komlan_Mally" title="Komlan Mally">Komlan Mally</a> resigns as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Prime_minister_of_Togo" title="Prime minister of Togo">prime minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/Togo" title="Togo">Togo</a>, after less than a year in office. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2008-09/06/content_9806371.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Darren_Aronofsky" title="Darren Aronofsky">Darren Aronofsky</a>'s <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wrestler_(2008_film)" title="The Wrestler (2008 film)">The Wrestler</a></i> wins the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Lion" title="Golden Lion">Golden Lion</a> for best film at the <a href="/wiki/Venice_Film_Festival" title="Venice Film Festival">Venice Film Festival</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5ghYFThcBadzak8ULA-rG0YHCKACgD931CNCO0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a><sup class="noprint Inline-Template"><span style="white-space: nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot" title="Wikipedia:Link rot"><span title=" Dead link since October 2012">dead link</span></a></i>]</span></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nuclear_Suppliers_Group" title="Nuclear Suppliers Group">Nuclear Suppliers Group</a> clears <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indo-US_nuclear_deal" title="Indo-US nuclear deal">Indo-US nuclear deal</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ibnlive.com/news/nsg-clears-nuclear-waiver-for-india/73011-3.html?from=rssfeed" rel="nofollow">(CNN-IBN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Cairo_landslide" title="2008 Cairo landslide">2008 Cairo landslide</a>: At least 18 people are killed and 22 injured when dozens of homes in northern <a href="/wiki/Cairo" title="Cairo">Cairo</a> collapse after being hit by a massive <a href="/wiki/Rockslide" title="Rockslide">rockslide</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://afp.google.com/article/ALeqM5hlNrnTEEvD-4zLBYFWNTcilTUc6w" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/2008_Summer_Paralympics" title="2008 Summer Paralympics">2008 Summer Paralympic Games</a> begin in <a href="/wiki/Beijing" title="Beijing">Beijing</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport2/hi/other_sports/disability_sport/7599977.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2008 Atlantic hurricane season">2008 Atlantic hurricane season</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Hanna_(2008)" title="Hurricane Hanna (2008)">Tropical Storm Hanna</a> makes landfall in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> on the border between <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">North Carolina</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Carolina" title="South Carolina">South Carolina</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theage.com.au/world/hanna-hits-us-coast-20080906-4az3.html?page=-1" rel="nofollow">(AFP via the <i>Melbourne Age</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike_(2008)" title="Hurricane Ike (2008)">Hurricane Ike</a> reaches Category 4 strength as it prepares to hit <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos" title="Turks and Caicos">Turks and Caicos</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5g918hbtK02_PM8gtnv_-6UZu8yEAD931FDUG0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a><sup class="noprint Inline-Template"><span style="white-space: nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Link_rot" title="Wikipedia:Link rot"><span title=" Dead link since October 2012">dead link</span></a></i>]</span></sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Electoral_College_of_Pakistan" title="Electoral College of Pakistan">Electoral College of Pakistan</a> elects <a href="/wiki/Asif_Ali_Zardari" title="Asif Ali Zardari">Asif Ali Zardari</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Peoples_Party" title="Pakistan Peoples Party">Pakistan Peoples Party</a> as the next <a href="/wiki/President_of_Pakistan" title="President of Pakistan">President of Pakistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/07/world/asia/07zardari.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Car_bomb" title="Car bomb">car bomb</a> in <a href="/wiki/Peshawar" title="Peshawar">Peshawar</a> in northwest Pakistan kills at least thirty people. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/7601671.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 7, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-07</span>)</span> (Sunday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_7&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_7&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_7&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/RENT" title="RENT">RENT</a> closed on <a href="/wiki/Broadway_theatre" title="Broadway theatre">Broadway</a>, leaving it the 7th longest running Broadway show, with its 12-year run, which began in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Serena_Williams" title="Serena Williams">Serena Williams</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Jelena_Jankovi%C4%87" title="Jelena Janković">Jelena Janković</a> to win the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_U.S._Open_-_Women%27s_Singles" title="2008 U.S. Open - Women's Singles">U.S. Open</a> for the third time, regaining the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_WTA_number_1_ranked_players" title="List of WTA number 1 ranked players">World Number 1 ranking</a> for the first time in five years. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/08/sports/tennis/08women.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike_(2008)" title="Hurricane Ike (2008)">Hurricane Ike</a> damages 80 percent of homes in the <a href="/wiki/Turks_and_Caicos_Islands" title="Turks and Caicos Islands">Turks and Caicos Islands</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.news.com.au/story/0,25197,24309666-2703,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Two <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bomber" title="Suicide bomber">suicide bombers</a> strike in the police headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Kandahar" title="Kandahar">Kandahar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> killing six officers and wounding several more. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iht.com/articles/2008/09/07/asia/afghan.php" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>International Herald Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_federal_government" title="United States federal government">United States federal government</a> places <a href="/wiki/Mortgage_loan" title="Mortgage loan">mortgage</a> financing companies <a href="/wiki/Freddie_Mac" title="Freddie Mac">Freddie Mac</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fannie_Mae" title="Fannie Mae">Fannie Mae</a> into <a href="/wiki/Conservatorship" title="Conservatorship">conservatorship</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Federal_Housing_Finance_Agency" title="Federal Housing Finance Agency">Federal Housing Finance Agency</a> will manage the companies on a temporary basis. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/businessNews/idINIndia-35361320080907" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Canadian Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Harper" title="Stephen Harper">Stephen Harper</a> has announced <a href="/wiki/Canadian_federal_election,_2008" title="Canadian federal election, 2008">an early election</a> scheduled for <a href="/wiki/October_14" title="October 14">October 14</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/7602864.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kurt_Beck" title="Kurt Beck">Kurt Beck</a>, the chairman of the <a href="/wiki/Social_Democratic_Party_of_Germany" title="Social Democratic Party of Germany">Social Democratic Party of Germany</a> steps down. According to media reports, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Frank_Walter_Steinmeier" title="Frank Walter Steinmeier">Frank Walter Steinmeier</a> will become the candidate for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chancellor_of_Germany_(Federal_Republic)" title="Chancellor of Germany (Federal Republic)">Chancellor of Germany</a> in the <a href="/wiki/German_federal_election,_2009" title="German federal election, 2009">2009 elections</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.tagesschau.de/inland/spd356.html" rel="nofollow">(ARD German)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Indian_Floods" title="2008 Indian Floods">Floods</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brahmaputra_river" title="Brahmaputra river">Brahmaputra river</a> have displaced estimated 2.1 <a href="/wiki/Million" title="Million">million</a> people and caused 24 deaths in north-eastern state of <a href="/wiki/Assam" title="Assam">Assam</a>, <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/India/Assam_flood_situation_grim_21_million_affected/rssarticleshow/3454633.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> go to the polls for the <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_legislative_election,_2008" title="Hong Kong legislative election, 2008">Hong Kong legislative election, 2008</a>. The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_Democratic_Alliance_for_the_Betterment_and_Progress_of_Hong_Kong" title="The Democratic Alliance for the Betterment and Progress of Hong Kong">Democratic Alliance</a> remains the largest party in the legislature. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2008-09/07/content_9820703.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601087&amp;sid=auQZjLHI192c&amp;refer=home" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Xinhua" title="Xinhua">Xinhua</a> reports that 20 people are trapped in a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coal_mine" title="Coal mine">coal mine</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Henan" title="Henan">Henan</a> province of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> following flooding. <a class="external text" href="http://www.charlotteobserver.com/world/story/177892.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Charlotte Observer</i>)</a></li>
<li>Vineet Raj Srivastava, The top Developer of HP India died</li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 8, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-08</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_8&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_8&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Popular_Movement_for_the_Liberation_of_Angola" title="Popular Movement for the Liberation of Angola">Popular Movement for the Liberation of Angola</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/Angolan_legislative_election,_2008" title="Angolan legislative election, 2008">2008 legislative election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/09/world/africa/09briefs-GOVERNINGPAR_BRF.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Roger_Federer" title="Roger Federer">Roger Federer</a> defeats <a href="/wiki/Andy_Murray" title="Andy Murray">Andy Murray</a> to win the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_U.S._Open_-_Men%27s_Singles" title="2008 U.S. Open - Men's Singles">U.S. Tennis Open</a> for a record-breaking fifth consecutive time. <a class="external text" href="http://msn.foxsports.com/tennis/story/8539492" rel="nofollow">(Fox Sports)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Washington_Mutual" title="Washington Mutual">Washington Mutual</a>, the largest <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Savings_and_loan" title="Savings and loan">savings and loan</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>, ousts <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chief_Executive" title="Chief Executive">Chief Executive</a> <a href="/wiki/Kerry_Killinger" title="Kerry Killinger">Kerry Killinger</a> as a result of losses incurred as a result of the <a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">subprime mortgage crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://dealbook.blogs.nytimes.com/2008/09/08/chief-forced-out-at-washington-mutual/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Landslide" title="Landslide">landslide</a> triggered by heavy rain strikes a <a href="/wiki/Warehouse" title="Warehouse">warehouse</a> in <a href="/wiki/Linfen" title="Linfen">Linfen</a> in <a href="/wiki/Shanxi" title="Shanxi">Shanxi</a> province, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>, killing at least 26 people and injuring others. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/world/story/2008/09/08/china-landslide.html" rel="nofollow">(Canadian Press)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike_(2008)" title="Hurricane Ike (2008)">Hurricane Ike</a> makes landfall near <a href="/wiki/Banes,_Cuba" title="Banes, Cuba">Banes</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, and weakens. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sunherald.com/218/story/798202.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Biloxi Sun Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/US_military" title="US military">US military</a> is to 'review an inquiry' into an air raid on a village in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Herat_province" title="Herat province">Herat province</a>, <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>, after a new video evidence emerged indicating 'scores of <a href="/wiki/Civilian" title="Civilian">civilian</a> deaths'. The US air raid in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> left up to 90 people dead, 'many of them women and children', the Afghan government and the UN said. However, US officials claimed earlier that 'no more than seven civilians died'. The bodies of 'at least 10 children and many more adults' appear in two videos made with cell phones in the <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghan</a> village <a href="/wiki/Azizabad,_Herat" title="Azizabad, Herat">Azizabad</a> after the raid. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/7603969.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://hosted.ap.org/dynamic/stories/A/AFGHAN_CIVILIAN_DEATHS?SITE=VASTR&amp;SECTION=HOME&amp;TEMPLATE=DEFAULT" rel="nofollow">(AP)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_South_Ossetia_war" title="2008 South Ossetia war">2008 South Ossetia war</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Russia" title="President of Russia">President of Russia</a> <a href="/wiki/Dmitry_Medvedev" title="Dmitry Medvedev">Dmitry Medvedev</a> and <a href="/wiki/President_of_France" title="President of France">President of France</a> <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Sarkozy" title="Nicolas Sarkozy">Nicolas Sarkozy</a> announced after talks in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> that an agreement to pull <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Russian_Federation" title="Armed Forces of the Russian Federation">Russian forces</a> from <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> within a month has been reached. The agreement has become possible as EU will send 200 civilian monitors to the area and guarantee that <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> signs a pledge to not use military force in <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> again. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSL272497420080908?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=worldNews&amp;pageNumber=3&amp;virtualBrandChannel=0" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.theglobeandmail.com/servlet/story/RTGAM.20080908.wrussia0908/BNStory/International/?page=rss&amp;id=RTGAM.20080908.wrussia0908" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Globe and Mail</i>)</a></li>
<li>'Senior <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army" title="United States Army">US soldiers</a> and two military contractors' were training 80 <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgian</a> <a href="/wiki/Special_forces" title="Special forces">special forces</a> serviceman only 'month prior' these commandos entered <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> on the night of August 8. <a href="/wiki/Military_Professional_Resources_Inc." title="Military Professional Resources Inc.">Military Professional Resources Inc.</a> (MPRI), one of the contractors, is known also for training the Croatian military in 1995 'prior to their invasion of the ethnically-<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Serbian_Krajina" title="Serbian Krajina">Serbian Krajina</a> region, which led to the displacement of 200,000 <a href="/wiki/Refugee" title="Refugee">refugees</a>'. However, 'there is no evidence' that the contractors or <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/US_military" title="US military">US military</a> knew these commandos 'were likely be used in the assault on South Ossetia'. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ft.com/cms/s/0/bdffd9a6-7b71-11dd-b839-000077b07658.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Financial Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Three <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> Muslim men are found guilty of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Conspiracy_(crime)" title="Conspiracy (crime)">conspiracy</a> to <a href="/wiki/Murder" title="Murder">murder</a> relating to the <a href="/wiki/2006_transatlantic_aircraft_plot" title="2006 transatlantic aircraft plot">2006 transatlantic aircraft plot</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/news/uk/crime/article4707468.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/UNITA" title="UNITA">UNITA</a> accepts defeat in the <a href="/wiki/Angolan_legislative_election,_2008" title="Angolan legislative election, 2008">Angolan legislative election, 2008</a>, the first parliamentary elections in <a href="/wiki/Angola" title="Angola">Angola</a> in 16 years, in which the ruling <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Popular_Movement_for_the_Liberation_of_Angola" title="Popular Movement for the Liberation of Angola">Popular Movement for the Liberation of Angola</a> wins more than 80% of the votes. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/7605454.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Al_Franken" title="Al Franken">Al Franken</a> wins a <a href="/wiki/Primary_election" title="Primary election">primary election</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Minnesota_Democratic%E2%80%93Farmer%E2%80%93Labor_Party" title="Minnesota Democratic–Farmer–Labor Party">Minnesota Democratic–Farmer–Labor Party</a> to challenge incumbent <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_of_the_United_States" title="Senate of the United States">Senator</a> <a href="/wiki/Norm_Coleman" title="Norm Coleman">Norm Coleman</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate_election_in_Minnesota,_2008" title="United States Senate election in Minnesota, 2008">Minnesota Senate election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5hvonEK0aSFP9aZpT3p6uUTlUQ_GwD933IPH81" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_of_Sri_Lanka" title="Military of Sri Lanka">military of Sri Lanka</a> declares 12 of its soldiers and one policeman killed in a suicide attack by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tamil_Tigers" title="Tamil Tigers">Tamil Tigers</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mullaittivu" title="Mullaittivu">Mullaittivu</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/7605498.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Malaysia" title="Prime Minister of Malaysia">Prime Minister of Malaysia</a> <a href="/wiki/Abdullah_Ahmad_Badawi" title="Abdullah Ahmad Badawi">Abdullah Ahmad Badawi</a> states that the governing <a href="/wiki/United_Malays_National_Organisation" title="United Malays National Organisation">United Malays National Organisation</a> (UMNO) will punish <a href="/wiki/Ahmad_Ismail_(Malaysian_politician)" title="Ahmad Ismail (Malaysian politician)">Ahmad Ismail</a>, a party official, for a series of statements he made about <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysia</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Malaysian_Chinese" title="Malaysian Chinese">ethnic Chinese</a> population. <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB122096793343314743.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> decides to withdraw aid workers from <a href="/wiki/Liberation_Tigers_of_Tamil_Eelam" title="Liberation Tigers of Tamil Eelam">Tamil Tiger</a>-held areas of <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/7606864.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike" title="Hurricane Ike">Hurricane Ike</a> makes its second landfall on <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, near <a href="/wiki/San_Crist%C3%B3bal,_Cuba" title="San Cristóbal, Cuba">San Cristóbal</a>, north of the <a href="/wiki/Isla_de_la_Juventud" title="Isla de la Juventud">Isle of Youth</a>, on its way into the <a href="/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico" title="Gulf of Mexico">Gulf of Mexico</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2008/US/weather/09/09/hurricane.ike/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> court rules that <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Thailand" title="Prime Minister of Thailand">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Samak_Sundaravej" title="Samak Sundaravej">Samak Sundaravej</a> must be removed from office for receiving payment for appearing on a television <a href="/wiki/Cooking_show" title="Cooking show">cooking show</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5hG71oGl1LokvZphtDQZzL44nzc3QD933CQI80" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>US President <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> pledges 4,500 troops to <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a> over the next few months and orders 8,000 troops currently stationed in <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> to be home by February. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/world/story/2008/09/09/iraq-bush.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Apple_Inc." title="Apple Inc.">Apple Inc.</a> unveils the revamped <a href="/wiki/IPod" title="IPod">iPod</a> line-up including the redesigned, fourth-generation <a href="/wiki/IPod_Nano" title="IPod Nano">iPod Nano</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/musicNews/idUSN0929983020080909" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Georgian opposition members demand <a href="/wiki/President_of_Georgia" title="President of Georgia">President of Georgia</a> <a href="/wiki/Mikheil_Saakashvili" title="Mikheil Saakashvili">Mikheil Saakashvili</a>'s resignation. Saakashvili believes he will "survive the crisis politically". <a class="external text" href="http://www.washingtonpost.com/wp-dyn/content/article/2008/09/08/AR2008090802449_pf.html" rel="nofollow">(Washington Post)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.newstin.com/tag/us/76513010" rel="nofollow">(Newstin)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_10&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2008" title="United States presidential election, 2008">United States presidential election, 2008</a>: Former <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> <a href="/wiki/Ron_Paul_presidential_campaign,_2008" title="Ron Paul presidential campaign, 2008">candidate</a> <a href="/wiki/Ron_Paul" title="Ron Paul">Ron Paul</a> endorses <a href="/wiki/Third_party_(United_States)" title="Third party (United States)">third-party</a> candidates <a href="/wiki/Chuck_Baldwin" title="Chuck Baldwin">Chuck Baldwin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bob_Barr" title="Bob Barr">Bob Barr</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cynthia_McKinney" title="Cynthia McKinney">Cynthia McKinney</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ralph_Nader" title="Ralph Nader">Ralph Nader</a>, calling the <a href="/wiki/Two-party_system" title="Two-party system">two-party system</a> a "charade."<a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/news/politics/la-na-thirdparty11-2008sep11,0,1874271.story" rel="nofollow">(Los Angeles Times)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_Bolivia" title="President of Bolivia">President of Bolivia</a> <a href="/wiki/Evo_Morales" title="Evo Morales">Evo Morales</a> expels the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a href="/wiki/Ambassador" title="Ambassador">ambassador</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philip_Goldberg" title="Philip Goldberg">Philip Goldberg</a>, for allegedly encouraging anti-government protests. <a class="external text" href="http://cbs2chicago.com/national/bolivia.us.ambassador.2.814449.html" rel="nofollow">(CBS)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/OPEC" title="OPEC">OPEC</a> announces it will cut oil production by 500,000 barrels a day; prices rise accordingly. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5i5TtajgUpSm7KY5jf-lCJGHBB-tAD933LA780" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S." title="U.S.">U.S.</a>-based financial services company <a href="/wiki/Lehman_Brothers" title="Lehman Brothers">Lehman Brothers</a> announces a third-quarter loss of <a href="/wiki/United_States_dollar" title="United States dollar">$</a>4.9 billion and plans to sell assets. <a class="external text" href="http://money.cnn.com/2008/09/10/news/newsmakers/lehman_fuld.fortune/index.htm" rel="nofollow">(CNN Money)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/European_Commission" title="European Commission">European Commission</a> predicts the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.K." title="U.K.">U.K.</a>, <a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">Germany</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">Spain</a> 'to fall into recession'; the outlook for rest of the <a href="/wiki/Eurozone" title="Eurozone">Eurozone</a> is gloomy. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/business/7607920.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Yonhap" title="Yonhap">Yonhap</a> News Agency in <a href="/wiki/South_Korea" title="South Korea">South Korea</a> reports <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korean</a> leader <a href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-il" title="Kim Jong-il">Kim Jong-il</a> has a serious health problem. <a class="external text" href="http://afp.google.com/article/ALeqM5j2zReXndGtxbEQ9gsY3SWxImKHHw" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a>
<ul>
<li>Western intelligence officials say Kim Jong-il might have suffered a stroke.<a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/7607513.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.npr.org/templates/story/story.php?storyId=94449410" rel="nofollow">(NPR)</a>, which North Korea denies. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/topNews/idUSSEO30199920080910" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/CERN" title="CERN">CERN</a> successfully circulates a beam through the entire <a href="/wiki/Large_Hadron_Collider" title="Large Hadron Collider">Large Hadron Collider</a> for the first time. <a class="external text" href="http://www.wired.com/science/discoveries/multimedia/2008/09/gallery_cern" rel="nofollow">(Wired)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://blog.wired.com/wiredscience/2008/09/first-beam-circ.html" rel="nofollow">(Wired)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_South_Ossetia_war" title="2008 South Ossetia war">2008 South Ossetia war</a>:
<ul>
<li>Some members of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_Committee_on_Foreign_Affairs" title="United States House Committee on Foreign Affairs">United States House Committee on Foreign Affairs</a> have expressed disagreement with Georgia's actions in the war: 'The recent fighting [...] was started by <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>. The Georgians broke the truce, not the <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russians</a>' said <a href="/wiki/Dana_Rohrabacher" title="Dana Rohrabacher">Dana Rohrabacher</a>, Senior Republican. <a class="external text" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=vIZu-rLLtlY" rel="nofollow">(RT via YouTube)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.russiatoday.com/news/news/30197" rel="nofollow">(RT)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 11, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-11</span>)</span> (Thursday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_11&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_11&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_11&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ayman_al-Zawahiri" title="Ayman al-Zawahiri">Ayman al-Zawahiri</a>, number two leader of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al_Qaeda" title="Al Qaeda">al Qaeda</a>, questions <a href="/wiki/Abu_Ayyub_al-Masri" title="Abu Ayyub al-Masri">Abu Ayyub al-Masri</a>'s ability to lead <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Al_Qaeda_in_Iraq" title="Al Qaeda in Iraq">al Qaeda in Iraq</a>, and accuses that organization's umbrella group, the <a href="/wiki/Islamic_State_of_Iraq" title="Islamic State of Iraq">Islamic State of Iraq</a>, of lying to the media about its activities. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/meast/09/11/alqaeda.letters/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Prices for <a href="/wiki/Petroleum" title="Petroleum">oil</a> fall <a class="external text" href="http://money.cnn.com/2008/09/11/markets/oil/index.htm" rel="nofollow">(CNN Money)</a>, and wholesale prices for <a href="/wiki/Gasoline" title="Gasoline">gasoline</a> rise sharply. <a class="external text" href="http://money.cnn.com/2008/09/11/news/economy/gas_prices/index.htm" rel="nofollow">(CNN Money)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_unrest_in_Bolivia" title="2008 unrest in Bolivia">2008 unrest in Bolivia</a>:
<ul>
<li>Fresh violence in <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a> stokes <a href="/wiki/Civil_war" title="Civil war">civil war</a> fears. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/Fresh_violence_in_Bolivia_stokes_civil_war_fears/articleshow/3472988.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/President_of_Venezuela" title="President of Venezuela">President of Venezuela</a> <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a> gives the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> ambassador 72 hours to leave <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> in part to show solidarity with the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Bolivia" title="President of Bolivia">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Evo_Morales" title="Evo Morales">Evo Morales</a> who recently expelled the U.S. ambassador to <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a>, accusing the U.S. of supporting protests against Morales. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5iXp7kZBY1LarAJ4_qn0KwWPOwznQD934RE700" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Morgan_Tsvangirai" title="Morgan Tsvangirai">Morgan Tsvangirai</a>, the leader of the <a href="/wiki/Movement_for_Democratic_Change_%E2%80%93_Tsvangirai" title="Movement for Democratic Change – Tsvangirai">Movement for Democratic Change</a>, claims that a power sharing agreement has been reached with the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/President_of_Zimbabwe" title="President of Zimbabwe">President of Zimbabwe</a> <a href="/wiki/Robert_Mugabe" title="Robert Mugabe">Robert Mugabe</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/7611459.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Officials order the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Galveston_Evacuation" title="2008 Galveston Evacuation">evacuation</a> of <a href="/wiki/Galveston_Island" title="Galveston Island">Galveston Island</a> in the U.S. state of <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a> before <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike_(2008)" title="Hurricane Ike (2008)">Hurricane Ike</a> makes landfall later in the week. <a class="external text" href="http://blogs.usatoday.com/ondeadline/2008/09/galveston-order.html?csp=34" rel="nofollow">(<i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> is reported to have authorized <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> special forces to conduct operations against insurgents inside Pakistan without seeking approval from the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Pakistan" title="Government of Pakistan">Government of Pakistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/POLITICS/09/11/us.pakistan.raids/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>A new survey of residents of 17 countries by <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=WorldPublicOpinion.org&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="WorldPublicOpinion.org (page does not exist)">WorldPublicOpinion.org</a> indicates that an average of 46 percent believe that <a href="/wiki/Al-Qaeda" title="Al-Qaeda">Al-Qaeda</a> was behind the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/9/11_attacks" title="9/11 attacks">9/11 attacks</a> of 2001. <a class="external text" href="http://english.aljazeera.net/news/americas/2008/09/200891133339749344.html" rel="nofollow">(Al Jazeera)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.voanews.com/english/2008-09-10-voa59.cfm" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.upi.com/Top_News/2008/09/11/Al-Qaida_not_universally_blamed_for_911/UPI-82141221114132/" rel="nofollow">(UPI)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://in.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idINIndia-35417520080910" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Two <a href="/wiki/Russian_Air_Force" title="Russian Air Force">Russian Air Force</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tu-160" title="Tu-160">Tu-160</a> bombers arrive in <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a> to carry out training flights over a course of several days. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/7609577.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Richter_magnitude_scale" title="Richter magnitude scale">6.6 magnitude</a> <a href="/wiki/Earthquake" title="Earthquake">earthquake</a> hits near <a href="/wiki/Ternate" title="Ternate">Ternate</a>, <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesia</a>, followed by a 7.2 magnitude quake near <a href="/wiki/Hokkaido" title="Hokkaido">Hokkaido</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/in_depth/7609574.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Forty people go missing in the northern <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indian_state" title="Indian state">Indian state</a> of <a href="/wiki/Bihar" title="Bihar">Bihar</a> after a boat capsizes in the Harohar River. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5jONv6Ee55aD3HCYLlOAH2SACSPGwD934B2FG0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/2008_Channel_Tunnel_fire" title="2008 Channel Tunnel fire">fire occurs</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Channel_Tunnel" title="Channel Tunnel">Channel Tunnel</a> and the tunnel is closed until further notice. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/europe/7610919.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Pentagon_Memorial" title="Pentagon Memorial">Pentagon Memorial</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington,_DC" title="Washington, DC">Washington, DC</a>, dedicated to the 184 people who died in the attack on the building on <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/September_11,_2001" title="September 11, 2001">September 11, 2001</a>, is opened to the public. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/Politics/story?id=5777731&amp;page=1" rel="nofollow">(ABC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
