<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Northwest_Orient_Airlines_Flight_2501" title="Northwest Orient Airlines Flight 2501">Northwest Orient Airlines Flight 2501</a>: Fifty years after the airliner vanished over <a href="/wiki/Lake_Michigan" title="Lake Michigan">Lake Michigan</a>, it is claimed that human remains washed ashore and were buried without the relatives' knowledge in an unmarked mass grave.<a class="external text" href="http://www.freep.com/apps/pbcs.dll/article?AID=/20080912/NEWS06/80912022/1008/NEWS" rel="nofollow">(Detroit Free Press)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_unrest_in_Bolivia" title="2008 unrest in Bolivia">2008 unrest in Bolivia</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a> declares <a href="/wiki/Martial_law" title="Martial law">martial law</a> in the department of <a href="/wiki/Pando_Department" title="Pando Department">Pando</a> following days of clashes between supporters of the national and local governments. <a class="external text" href="http://afp.google.com/article/ALeqM5ji6H18az0aIKyD5jHaC6j3sawCAg" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/hi/spanish/latin_america/newsid_7613000/7613726.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC Mundo)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Honduras" title="Honduras">Honduran</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_Honduras" title="President of Honduras">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Manuel_Zelaya" title="Manuel Zelaya">Manuel Zelaya</a> tells the incoming <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">U.S.</a> ambassador not to present his credentials in a show of solidarity with <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://uk.reuters.com/article/oilRpt/idUKN1240144420080912" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The collapse of the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>'s third largest tour operator <a href="/wiki/XL_Leisure_Group" title="XL Leisure Group">XL Leisure Group</a>, leaves over 85,000 British holidaymakers stranded abroad. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/business/7611639.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
<li>Twenty Four people die in <a href="/wiki/Chatsworth,_Los_Angeles" title="Chatsworth, Los Angeles">Chatsworth</a> in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> <a href="/wiki/2008_Chatsworth_train_collision" title="2008 Chatsworth train collision">following a collision</a> between a <a href="/wiki/Metrolink_(California)" title="Metrolink (California)">Metrolink</a> passenger train and a <a href="/wiki/Union_Pacific_Railroad" title="Union Pacific Railroad">Union Pacific</a> freight train. At least 135 people were also injured in the accident. <a class="external text" href="http://www.latimes.com/news/local/la-me-traincrash13-2008sep13,0,2874450.story" rel="nofollow">(Los Angeles Times)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.sfgate.com/cgi-bin/article.cgi?f=/n/a/2008/09/12/national/a201133D68.DTL" rel="nofollow">(San Francisco Chronicle)</a></li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/Car_bomb" title="Car bomb">car bomb</a> in the mainly <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Shiite" title="Shiite">Shiite</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Dujail" title="Dujail">Dujail</a> in <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> kills at least 32 people and injures another 43. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/stories/2008/09/12/iraq/main4445165.shtml" rel="nofollow">(AP via CBS News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Thailand" title="Thailand">Thai</a> <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Power_Party_(Thailand)" title="People's Power Party (Thailand)">People's Power Party</a> agrees not to renominate ousted <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Thailand" title="Prime Minister of Thailand">Prime Minister of Thailand</a> <a href="/wiki/Samak_Sundaravej" title="Samak Sundaravej">Samak Sundaravej</a> for the position following objections from the other members of the coalition. <a class="external text" href="http://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory?id=5785479" rel="nofollow">(AP via ABC News America)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Army" title="Pakistan Army">Pakistan Army</a> claims that at least 30 militants and 2 soldiers have been killed in fighting in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bajaur" title="Bajaur">Bajaur</a> region of the <a href="/wiki/Federally_Administered_Tribal_Areas" title="Federally Administered Tribal Areas">Federally Administered Tribal Areas</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5jIE0IUn4WIiaMBpjG8SI_6H5RXzgD93507A80" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Malaysia" title="Malaysia">Malaysian</a> government arrests the editor and prominent blogger activist <a href="/wiki/Raja_Petra_Kamarudin" title="Raja Petra Kamarudin">Raja Petra Kamarudin</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Malaysia_Today" title="Malaysia Today">Malaysia Today</a> website, a journalist from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sin_Chew_Jit_Poh" title="Sin Chew Jit Poh">Sin Chew Jit Poh</a> and opposition politician <a href="/wiki/Teresa_Kok" title="Teresa Kok">Teresa Kok</a> under the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Internal_Security_Act_(Malaysia)" title="Internal Security Act (Malaysia)">Internal Security Act</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/7612666.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.malaysiakini.com/news/89602" rel="nofollow">(Malaysiakini)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.thestar.com.my/news/story.asp?file=/2008/9/12/nation/20080912221723&amp;sec=nation" rel="nofollow">(TheStar Online)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>-led coalition claims to kill at least 10 militants in fighting in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5ijDA5bgxiHlTvS_r-SSjskS1Tq1wD935059G0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_New_Zealand" title="Prime Minister of New Zealand">Prime Minister of New Zealand</a> <a href="/wiki/Helen_Clark" title="Helen Clark">Helen Clark</a> calls an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Zealand_general_election_2008" title="New Zealand general election 2008">election</a> for <a href="/wiki/November_8" title="November 8">November 8</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/heraldsun/story/0,21985,24334188-661,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Melbourne Herald Sun)</a></li>
<li>North Korean leader <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kim_Jong-Il" title="Kim Jong-Il">Kim Jong-Il</a> is said by Chinese authorities to be suffering irregular convulsions following a stroke which kept him from attending the country's 60th anniversary celebration. Chinese authorities believe his long-term ability to govern will be impeded. <a class="external text" href="http://afp.google.com/article/ALeqM5idUb45NfGmaShZuitfgd3dh_-rdg" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Constitutional_Court_of_Spain" title="Constitutional Court of Spain">Constitutional Court of Spain</a> rules that the Government of the <a href="/wiki/Basque_Country_(autonomous_community)" title="Basque Country (autonomous community)">Basque Country</a> could not call a <a href="/wiki/Basque_referendum,_2008" title="Basque referendum, 2008">planned referendum</a> on working towards <a href="/wiki/Self-determination" title="Self-determination">self-determination</a> as only the <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Spain" title="Government of Spain">Government of Spain</a> could call such a vote; the Basque Government said it would appeal to the <a href="/wiki/European_Court_of_Human_Rights" title="European Court of Human Rights">European Court of Human Rights</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iht.com/articles/ap/2008/09/12/europe/EU-Spain-Basque-Referendum.php" rel="nofollow">(IHT)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<li>The death toll from the <a href="/wiki/2008_Chatsworth_train_collision" title="2008 Chatsworth train collision">2008 Chatsworth train collision</a> in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a> rises to 24 with more fatalities expected. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alertnet.org/thenews/newsdesk/N13412213.htm" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/13_September_2008_Delhi_bombings" title="13 September 2008 Delhi bombings">Five explosions</a> rock various places in <a href="/wiki/Delhi" title="Delhi">Delhi</a>, killing at least 30 people. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/India/Serial_blasts_rock_Delhi_several_injured/articleshow/3479914.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>India Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike_(2008)" title="Hurricane Ike (2008)">Hurricane Ike</a>:
<ul>
<li>Hurricane Ike makes landfall in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> at <a href="/wiki/Galveston,_Texas" title="Galveston, Texas">Galveston</a>, <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a>, as a Category 2 hurricane. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601087&amp;sid=agoQ2nrz6TVM&amp;refer=home" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li>Hurricane Ike weakens to a tropical storm over eastern Texas. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nola.com/hurricane-ike/index.ssf/2008/09/ike_weakens_to_a_tropical_stor.html" rel="nofollow">(National Hurricane Center via Nola.com)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> declares that Texas is a disaster zone. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/7614826.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>As many as one million <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">Haitians</a> become homeless due to <a href="/wiki/2008_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2008 Atlantic hurricane season">hurricanes</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/7613851.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Abullah Wardak, the Governor of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lowgar_Province" title="Lowgar Province">Lowgar Province</a> of <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>, is assassinated in a car bomb. <a class="external text" href="http://afp.google.com/article/ALeqM5gGGVG6fpG6Fx_NJBnLUnXOBwnx2g" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Shanxi_mudslide" title="2008 Shanxi mudslide">A mudslide</a> caused by an illegal mine in <a href="/wiki/Shanxi" title="Shanxi">Shanxi</a> province in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> kills 254 people. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2008-09/12/content_9950331.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua News Agency)</a></li>
<li>A bus crashes into a 100 m gorge in <a href="/wiki/Sichuan" title="Sichuan">Sichuan</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a>, killing 51. <a class="external text" href="http://www.zeenews.com/articles.asp?aid=468903&amp;sid=WOR" rel="nofollow">(Zee News)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/All_Blacks" title="All Blacks">All Blacks</a> defeat <a href="/wiki/Australia_national_rugby_union_team" title="Australia national rugby union team">Australia</a> (28–24) to win the <a href="/wiki/2008_Tri_Nations_Series" title="2008 Tri Nations Series">2008 Tri Nations Series</a> at the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suncorp_Stadium" title="Suncorp Stadium">Suncorp Stadium</a> in <a href="/wiki/Brisbane" title="Brisbane">Brisbane</a>, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.theage.com.au/sport/all-blacks-retain-trinations-bledisloe-20080913-4fyz.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Age</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_South_Ossetia_war" title="2008 South Ossetia war">2008 South Ossetia war</a>:
<ul>
<li>Russians troops leave west, but remain in Georgia. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5gDNLWfQWKrQc48pITBUg9KT_6oVwD936137G0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UNHCR" title="UNHCR">UNHCR</a>: around 192,000 people were forced to flee their homes in <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> during the four-day war of <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> with <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. Around 35 thousand of them left <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> shortly before August, 8th for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Ossetia" title="North Ossetia">North Ossetia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, others were forced to relocate during the conflict. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ptinews.com/pti%5Cptisite.nsf/0/746F711DE3078730652574C300267B8C?OpenDocument" rel="nofollow">(Press Trust of India)</a></li>
<li>A US Defense Department team to arrive in Georgia. <a class="external text" href="http://rustavi2.com/news/news_text.php?id_news=27875&amp;pg=1&amp;im=main&amp;ct=0&amp;wth=" rel="nofollow">(Rustavi 2)</a></li>
<li>Russian Foreign Minister <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Lavrov" title="Sergey Lavrov">Sergey Lavrov</a> said Saturday that Abkhazia and <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> cannot legally join the <a href="/wiki/Collective_Security_Treaty_Organization" title="Collective Security Treaty Organization">Collective Security Treaty Organization</a> (CSTO) due to their status, local press reported. <a class="external text" href="http://news.xinhuanet.com/english/2008-09/07/content_9817284.htm" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>Western countries are pledging substantial aid to Georgia – as much as 3.5-4 billion dollars in grants and loans. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rp.pl/artykul/172846,189329_The_true_price_of_war_in_Georgia_.html" rel="nofollow">(RP)</a></li>
<li>Georgia's President <a href="/wiki/Mikheil_Saakashvili" title="Mikheil Saakashvili">Mikheil Saakashvili</a> has arrived in the village of <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Koda,_Georgia&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Koda, Georgia (page does not exist)">Koda</a> and to supervise rehabilitation works of ten blocks, owned by the Georgian Defense ministry, in which the IDPs from South Ossetia will be temporarily settled there. <a class="external text" href="http://rustavi2.com/news/news_text.php?id_news=27876&amp;pg=1&amp;im=main&amp;ct=0&amp;wth=" rel="nofollow">(Rustavi 2)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_14&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_South_Ossetia_war" title="2008 South Ossetia war">2008 South Ossetia war</a>:
<ul>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Georgian_foreign_ministry" title="Georgian foreign ministry">Georgian foreign ministry</a> has released an official statement stating that 'In the villages of the Tskhinvali region/South Ossetia, Georgia, the separatist regime continues carrying out persecution of local Georgian population based on their ethnic origin', adding that 'Once again it becomes evident that for the Russian government the ethnic cleansing remains as one of the main methods for achieving its political goals'. <a class="external text" href="http://rustavi2.com/news/news_text.php?id_news=27881&amp;pg=1&amp;im=main&amp;ct=0&amp;wth=" rel="nofollow">(Rustavi 2)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dick_Cheney" title="Dick Cheney">Dick Cheney</a> on his visit to <a href="/wiki/Tbilisi" title="Tbilisi">Tbilisi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia (country)</a> earlier condemned Russian "invasion" and said that United States was "fully committed" to <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a>'s efforts to join <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/US-Vice-President-Dick-Cheney-Pledges-Support-To-Georgias-Mikheil-Saakashvili-On-Visit-To-Tbilisi/Article/200809115092985?lpos=World%2BNews_7&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15092985_US%2BVice%2BPresident%2BDick%2BCheney%2BPledges%2BSupport%2BTo%2BGeorgia%2527s%2BMikheil%2BSaakashvili%2BOn%2BVisit%2BTo%2BTbilisi" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> forces have pulled out of the Black Sea port of <a href="/wiki/Poti" title="Poti">Poti</a> and are preparing to withdraw from positions in western Georgia. <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russian</a> forces are to withdraw completely from <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> proper to an October 10 deadline. <a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">EU</a> foreign policy chief <a href="/wiki/Javier_Solana" title="Javier Solana">Javier Solana</a> said he was confident this deadline would be met. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/topNews/idUSLD28294220080913?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=topNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.iht.com/articles/reuters/2008/09/13/europe/OUKWD-UK-GEORGIA-OSSETIA-PULLOUT.php" rel="nofollow">(<i>The International Herald Tribune</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Russian-Troops-Said-To-Be-Withdrawing-From-Georgian-Black-Sea-Port-Of-Poti-And-Other-Areas/Article/200809215098711?lpos=World%2BNews_9&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15098711_Russian%2BTroops%2BSaid%2BTo%2BBe%2BWithdrawing%2BFrom%2BGeorgian%2BBlack%2BSea%2BPort%2BOf%2BPoti%2BAnd%2BOther%2BAreas" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Irakli_Okruashvili" title="Irakli Okruashvili">Irakli Okruashvili</a>, ex-defense minister of <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> granted political asylum in <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>, claims President of <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mikhail_Saakashvili" title="Mikhail Saakashvili">Mikhail Saakashvili</a> 'must be held accountable [for the war] and resign... If he doesn't it will lead to criminal charges against him'. Irakli Okruashvili claims he has been working with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mikhail_Saakashvili" title="Mikhail Saakashvili">Saakashvili</a> on plans to regain control on <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> since 2005 but was sure that <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> could not succeed by military means. <a class="external text" href="http://www.spiegel.de/international/world/0,1518,526493,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Spiegel)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.civil.ge/eng/article.php?id=19502" rel="nofollow">(Civil.Ge)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/American_International_Group" title="American International Group">American International Group</a> seeks an emergency $40 billion loan from the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Federal_Reserve" title="United States Federal Reserve">United States Federal Reserve</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://dealbook.blogs.nytimes.com/2008/09/14/aig-seeks-fed-aid-to-survive/index.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bank_of_America" title="Bank of America">Bank of America</a> negotiates to buy <a href="/wiki/Merrill_Lynch" title="Merrill Lynch">Merrill Lynch</a> for $38.25 billion in stock. <a class="external text" href="http://dealbook.blogs.nytimes.com/2008/09/14/bank-of-america-in-talks-to-buy-merrill-lynch/index.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB122142278543033525.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Federal_Reserve" title="United States Federal Reserve">United States Federal Reserve</a> announces several initiatives to expand emergency lending to combat the crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://www.startribune.com/business/28377589.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Minneapolis St-Paul Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lehman_Brothers" title="Lehman Brothers">Lehman Brothers</a> files for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chapter_11" title="Chapter 11">Chapter 11</a> <a href="/wiki/Bankruptcy" title="Bankruptcy">bankruptcy</a> after British bank <a href="/wiki/Barclays" title="Barclays">Barclays</a> and Bank of America pull out of emergency talks on a buyout. <a class="external text" href="http://afp.google.com/article/ALeqM5hxEeaW4uGo086bAifTpKwz-qW1Cw" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://dealbook.blogs.nytimes.com/2008/09/15/lehman-says-it-will-file-for-bankruptcy-2/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike" title="Hurricane Ike">Hurricane Ike</a>
<ul>
<li>Authorities in <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a> have rescued nearly 2,000 <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Ike_in_Texas" title="Effects of Hurricane Ike in Texas">victims of Hurricane Ike</a> who refused to evacuate. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5jG1m4XT341oCKXPMIZlKffdhP9vwD936LNM80" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">American</a> death toll from Hurricane Ike rises to 8. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/15/us/15ike.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nigerian_Oil_Crisis" title="Nigerian Oil Crisis">Nigerian Oil Crisis</a>: <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>'s main rebel group declared an "oil war" in the west African nation in response to what it said were "unprovoked" attacks by Nigerian government forces a day earlier. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/africa/09/14/nigeria.oil.war/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Shootout between police and unknown assailants leaves 20 police officers dead in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ashkhabad" title="Ashkhabad">Ashkhabad</a>, <a href="/wiki/Turkmenistan" title="Turkmenistan">Turkmenistan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.smh.com.au/world/twenty-police-killed-in-turkmenistan-20080914-4g1s.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Sydney Morning Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sebastian_Vettel" title="Sebastian Vettel">Sebastian Vettel</a> of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Toro_Rosso" title="Toro Rosso">Toro Rosso</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/2008_Italian_Grand_Prix" title="2008 Italian Grand Prix">2008 Italian Grand Prix</a> at <a href="/wiki/Autodromo_Nazionale_Monza" title="Autodromo Nazionale Monza">Monza</a>, becoming the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Formula_One_driver_records#Youngest_winners" title="List of Formula One driver records">youngest driver</a> in history to win a Formula One grand prix. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport1/hi/motorsport/formula_one/7615250.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Two people are killed and 10 injured when a tourist riverboat collides with a pillar of the <a href="/wiki/Pont_de_l%27Archev%C3%AAch%C3%A9" title="Pont de l'Archevêché">Pont de l'Archevêché</a> and sinks, on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/River_Seine" title="River Seine">River Seine</a> in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/france/2956536/Two-dead-in-Paris-tourist-boat.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Thai_political_crisis" title="2008 Thai political crisis">2008 Thai political crisis</a>: The Acting <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Thailand" title="Prime Minister of Thailand">Prime Minister of Thailand</a> <a href="/wiki/Somchai_Wongsawat" title="Somchai Wongsawat">Somchai Wongsawat</a> lifts a <a href="/wiki/State_of_emergency" title="State of emergency">state of emergency</a> in place since September 2. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/14/world/asia/14bangkok.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/National_Party_of_Western_Australia" title="National Party of Western Australia">National Party of Western Australia</a> indicates that it will support the <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_Australia" title="Liberal Party of Australia">Liberal Party of Australia</a> in forming a <a href="/wiki/Minority_government" title="Minority government">minority government</a> in <a href="/wiki/Western_Australia" title="Western Australia">Western Australia</a>. Liberal leader, <a href="/wiki/Colin_Barnett" title="Colin Barnett">Colin Barnett</a>, becomes the <a href="/wiki/Premier_of_Western_Australia" title="Premier of Western Australia">Premier-elect</a> and incumbent Premier <a href="/wiki/Alan_Carpenter" title="Alan Carpenter">Alan Carpenter</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Australian_Labor_Party" title="Australian Labor Party">Australian Labor Party</a> concedes defeat. <a class="external text" href="http://www.theaustralian.news.com.au/story/0,25197,24343987-12377,00.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Boeing_737" title="Boeing 737">Boeing 737</a> <a href="/wiki/Aeroflot_Flight_821" title="Aeroflot Flight 821">Aeroflot Flight 821</a> crashes near the city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Perm_(Russia)" title="Perm (Russia)">Perm</a> in <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>, killing all 88 on board. The cause of the crash is attributed to engine failure. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/7614951.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.chicagotribune.com/news/nationworld/sns-ap-russia-plane-crash,0,3299178.story" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Chicago Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_unrest_in_Bolivia" title="2008 unrest in Bolivia">2008 unrest in Bolivia</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a> suffers severe natural gas shortages following the cut off of natural gas supplies from Bolivia, which provides half of Brazil's natural gas. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ft.com/cms/s/0/651e2e9a-8063-11dd-99a9-000077b07658.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Financial Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Government officials announce they plan to arrest <a href="/wiki/Pando_Department" title="Pando Department">Pando</a> Governor <a href="/wiki/Leopoldo_Fern%C3%A1ndez" title="Leopoldo Fernández">Leopoldo Fernández</a> and that troops from Cobija airport will be sent to retake the city. <a class="external text" href="http://www.alertnet.org/thenews/newsdesk/N13400579.htm" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Accusations of <a href="/wiki/Witchcraft" title="Witchcraft">witchcraft</a> cause <a href="/wiki/2008_Congo_football_riots" title="2008 Congo football riots">football riots</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a>, resulting in 13 dead and 36 injured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/africaandindianocean/democraticrepublicofcongo/2962727/Eleven-dead-in-Congo-football-riot-after-use-of-witchcraft.html" rel="nofollow">(The Daily Telegraph)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>The government of <a href="/wiki/Samoa" title="Samoa">Samoa</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/International_reaction_to_the_2008_declaration_of_independence_by_Kosovo" title="International reaction to the 2008 declaration of independence by Kosovo">recognizes the independence</a> of <a href="/wiki/Kosovo" title="Kosovo">Kosovo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.newkosovareport.com/200809151219/Politics/Samoa-recognizes-indepedent-Kosovo.html" rel="nofollow">(New Kosova Report)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Morelia_Bomb_Attacks" title="2008 Morelia Bomb Attacks">Morelia Bomb Attacks</a>: Eight people are killed and 100 injured in a presumed <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Terrorist_attack" title="Terrorist attack">terrorist attack</a> at <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grito_de_Dolores" title="Grito de Dolores">El Grito</a></i> <a href="/wiki/Mexican_War_of_Independence" title="Mexican War of Independence">Independence Day</a> celebrations in the <a href="/wiki/Z%C3%B3calo" title="Zócalo">main square</a> of <a href="/wiki/Morelia" title="Morelia">Morelia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michoac%C3%A1n" title="Michoacán">Michoacán</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/7618824.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.eluniversal.com.mx/notas/538695.html" rel="nofollow">(El Universal)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Hewlett-Packard" title="Hewlett-Packard">Hewlett-Packard</a> announces plans to cut 24,600 jobs. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/newsOne/idUSWNAB125620080915" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Shots are fired into the air in a confrontation <a href="/wiki/Pakistan%E2%80%93United_States_relations" title="Pakistan–United States relations">between US and Pakistani forces</a>; US forces retreat; Pakistan denies involvement of their forces. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/south_asia/7396366.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jaap_de_Hoop_Scheffer" title="Jaap de Hoop Scheffer">Jaap de Hoop Scheffer</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Secretary_General_of_NATO" title="Secretary General of NATO">Secretary General of NATO</a>, visits <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> in a show of support. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/news/world/2008-09-15-georgia-nato_N.htm?csp=34" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>USA Today)</i></a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Richard_Wright_(musician)" title="Richard Wright (musician)">Richard Wright</a>, a founding member of the English rock group <a href="/wiki/Pink_Floyd" title="Pink Floyd">Pink Floyd</a>, dies at the age of 65 after a long battle with <a href="/wiki/Cancer" title="Cancer">cancer</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/SHOWBIZ/Music/09/15/obit.wright.ap/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>At least 11 spectators die in a <a href="/wiki/Stampede" title="Stampede">stampede</a> at a club <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> match in <a href="/wiki/Butembo" title="Butembo">Butembo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a>, following a riot incited when a <a href="/wiki/Goalkeeper" title="Goalkeeper">goalkeeper</a> used an <a href="/wiki/Animism" title="Animism">animist</a> spell in an attempt to rally his team. <a class="external text" href="http://soccernet.espn.go.com/news/story?id=572469&amp;sec=espn.com&amp;cc=5901" rel="nofollow">(Radio Okapi via ESPN)</a></li>
<li>Twelve tourists are killed and 37 injured when a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coach_(vehicle)" title="Coach (vehicle)">coach</a> collides with a delivery truck outside of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ras_Sidr" title="Ras Sidr">Ras Sidr</a> in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>. Reports suggest 7 of the 12 dead are foreign nationals. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Tourists-Dead-As-Coach-and-Truck-Crash-In-Egypt/Article/200809315099513?lpos=World%2BNews_4&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15099513_Tourists%2BDead%2BAs%2BCoach%2Band%2BTruck%2BCrash%2BIn%2BEgypt" rel="nofollow">(Sky News)</a></li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Zimbabwean_political_negotiations" title="2008 Zimbabwean political negotiations">power-sharing agreement</a> between <a href="/wiki/Zimbabwe" title="Zimbabwe">Zimbabwean</a> president <a href="/wiki/Robert_Mugabe" title="Robert Mugabe">Robert Mugabe</a> and opposition leader <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Tsvangirai" title="Morgan Tsvangirai">Morgan Tsvangirai</a> is officially signed, making Tsvangirai <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Zimbabwe" title="Prime Minister of Zimbabwe">Prime Minister of Zimbabwe</a> and chair of cabinet meetings. Mugabe maintains his position as president and remains in control of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Military_of_Zimbabwe" title="Military of Zimbabwe">the country's army</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/africaandindianocean/zimbabwe/2961901/Zimbabwe-leaders-Robert-Mugabe-and-Morgan-Tsvangirai-sign-power-sharing-deal.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nigerian_Oil_Crisis" title="Nigerian Oil Crisis">Nigerian Oil Crisis</a>: <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a>'s main rebel group claim to have destroyed an oil installation owned by <a href="/wiki/Royal_Dutch_Shell" title="Royal Dutch Shell">Shell</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Rivers_State" title="Rivers State">Rivers State</a> region in the south of the country. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/africa/7616165.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>A stampede in the <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">Indonesian</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Pasuruan" title="Pasuruan">Pasuruan</a> leaves 21 people dead, most of whom are thought to be women. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/asia-pacific/7616009.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>At least one person has died and 26 are missing after a <a href="/wiki/Roll-on/roll-off" title="Roll-on/roll-off">Ro-ro ferry</a> sinks near the <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkish</a> city of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bandirma" title="Bandirma">Bandirma</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.sky.com/skynews/Home/World-News/Turkey-Ferry-Sinks-Many-Missing-As-Boat-Goes-Down-Near-Port-Of-Bandirma/Article/200809315099344?lpos=World%2BNews_4&amp;lid=ARTICLE_15099344_Turkey%2BFerry%2BSinks%253A%2BMany%2BMissing%2BAs%2BBoat%2BGoes%2BDown%2BNear%2BPort%2BOf%2BBandirma" rel="nofollow">(<i>Sky News</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Lehman_Brothers" title="Lehman Brothers">Lehman Brothers</a> <a href="/wiki/Bankruptcy_of_Lehman_Brothers" title="Bankruptcy of Lehman Brothers">files</a> for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chapter_11" title="Chapter 11">Chapter 11</a> <a href="/wiki/Bankruptcy" title="Bankruptcy">bankruptcy</a> resulting from the subprime mortgage crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://dealbook.blogs.nytimes.com/2008/09/15/lehman-says-it-will-file-for-bankruptcy-2/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">Dow Jones Industrial Average</a> falls by over 500 points as the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Stock_Exchange" title="New York Stock Exchange">New York Stock Exchange</a> responds to events over the weekend. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/16/business/worldbusiness/16markets.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>Six men have been found guilty of terrorism-related offences in <a href="/wiki/Melbourne" title="Melbourne">Melbourne</a>, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. <a href="/wiki/Abdul_Nacer_Benbrika" title="Abdul Nacer Benbrika">Abdul Nacer Benbrika</a> was found guilty of intentionally directing the activities of a terrorist organization while five other men were found guilty of being members of the same organisation. Four other men were acquitted and the jury is still considering its verdict on two men. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2008/09/15/2364753.htm" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike_(2008)" title="Hurricane Ike (2008)">Hurricane Ike (2008)</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dd>
<ul>
<li>The remnants of Ike are blamed for 13 more deaths in the <a href="/wiki/Midwestern_United_States" title="Midwestern United States">Midwestern United States</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bostonherald.com/news/national/midwest/view/2008_09_15_Remnants_of_Ike_blamed_for_13_deaths_in_Midwest/srvc=home&amp;position=recent" rel="nofollow">(<i>Boston Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li>More than one million households in the Midwestern United States are left without electricity due to high winds. <a class="external text" href="http://dispatch.com/live/content/local_news/stories/2008/09/15/million.html?sid=101" rel="nofollow">(<i>Columbus Dispatch</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President</a> <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> warns that motorists will face a "pinch" from rising costs caused by Hurricane Ike. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/story/0,2933,422768,00.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
</ul>
</dd>
</dl>
<ul>
<li>NASA scientists report that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ozone_hole" title="Ozone hole">ozone hole</a> over the <a href="/wiki/Antarctic" title="Antarctic">Antarctic</a> has reached its largest expanse, 27 million square kilometers, vs 26 million square kilometers in 2006. <a class="external text" href="http://ozonewatch.gsfc.nasa.gov/" rel="nofollow">(NASA)</a> European Scientists at ESA concur. <a class="external autonumber" href="http://www.dailytech.com/article.aspx?newsid=13152" rel="nofollow">[1]</a></li>

<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_unrest_in_Bolivia" title="2008 unrest in Bolivia">Unrest in Bolivia</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Governor" title="Governor">Governor</a> of <a href="/wiki/Pando_Department" title="Pando Department">Pando</a> <a href="/wiki/Leopoldo_Fern%C3%A1ndez" title="Leopoldo Fernández">Leopoldo Fernández</a> is taken into custody by the armed forces, on charges of hiring hitmen to attack pro-government protesters. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/in_depth/7619853.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> organises at least two evacuation flights from <a href="/wiki/Bolivia" title="Bolivia">Bolivia</a> as the political situation worsens. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5hO82vQEsp5OkFPg3Kc0WAFbk4-pQD93817201" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/War_in_Somalia_(2006%E2%80%93present)" title="War in Somalia (2006–present)">Fighting in Somalia</a> has killed 838 people since June, according to local rights activists, bringing the total to have died in an insurgency that began early last year to 9,474. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reliefweb.int/rw/rwb.nsf/db900sid/AMMF-7JJCSY?OpenDocument" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Russian_financial_crisis" title="2008 Russian financial crisis">2008 Russian financial crisis</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s most liquid stock exchange <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MICEX" title="MICEX">MICEX</a> and the dollar-denominated <a href="/wiki/Russian_Trading_System" title="Russian Trading System">RTS</a> suspend trade for one hour after the worst one-day fall in ten years as Finance Minister <a href="/wiki/Alexei_Kudrin" title="Alexei Kudrin">Alexei Kudrin</a> reassured markets there was no "systemic" crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/rbssFinancialServicesAndRealEstateNews/idUSLG65392720080916" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a>: The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Federal_Reserve" title="United States Federal Reserve">United States Federal Reserve</a> agrees to lend the <a href="/wiki/American_International_Group" title="American International Group">American International Group</a> $85 billion in return for a 79.9% stake. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/17/business/17insure.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Six men have been found guilty of terrorism-related offences in <a href="/wiki/Melbourne" title="Melbourne">Melbourne</a>, <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">Australia</a>. <a href="/wiki/Abdul_Nacer_Benbrika" title="Abdul Nacer Benbrika">Abdul Nacer Benbrika</a> was found guilty of intentionally directing the activities of a terrorist organization while five other men were found guilty of being members of the same organization. Four other men were acquitted and the jury is still considering its verdict on two men. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2008/09/15/2364753.htm" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> government opens up a partnership with the <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Swedish</a> municipality of <a href="/wiki/S%C3%B6dert%C3%A4lje" title="Södertälje">Södertälje</a>, a city of 80,000 that has received nearly 6,000 <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraqi</a> refugees since the beginning of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Iraq_war" title="Iraq war">Iraq war</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thelocal.se/14370/20080916/" rel="nofollow">(The Local)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hamas-Fatah_conflict" title="Hamas-Fatah conflict">Hamas-Fatah conflict</a>: Fierce fighting between <a href="/wiki/Hamas" title="Hamas">Hamas</a> security forces and the pro-<a href="/wiki/Fatah" title="Fatah">Fatah</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Doghmush" title="Doghmush">Doghmush</a> organised crime family leaves 5 dead in <a href="/wiki/Gaza_City" title="Gaza City">Gaza City</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/middle_east/7618208.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Ukraine's ruling coalition is <a href="/wiki/2008_Ukrainian_political_crisis" title="2008 Ukrainian political crisis">formally dissolved</a> after parties supporting Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Yulia_Tymoshenko" title="Yulia Tymoshenko">Yulia Tymoshenko</a>, in alliance with the <a href="/wiki/Party_of_Regions" title="Party of Regions">Party of Regions</a>, pushed legislation limiting the powers of President <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Yushchenko" title="Viktor Yushchenko">Viktor Yushchenko</a> resulting in his party's withdrawal from the coalition. Tymoshenko's party is expected to form an alliance with the Party of Regions or new elections will be held. <a class="external text" href="http://afp.google.com/article/ALeqM5jtUOmlRyOSVtaxRetvox2V-OZ_fQ" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Viktor_Yushchenko" title="Viktor Yushchenko">Viktor Yushchenko</a> earlier accused pro-Western <a href="/wiki/Yulia_Tymoshenko" title="Yulia Tymoshenko">Yulia Tymoshenko</a> of committing a <a href="/wiki/High_treason" title="High treason">high treason</a> for not supporting <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> during the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_South_Ossetia_war" title="2008 South Ossetia war">2008 South Ossetia war</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://rawstory.com/news/afp/Ukraine_PM_refuses_to_resign_as_cri_09172008.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Rawstory)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/europe/ukraine/2706210/Ukraine-president-Viktor-Yushchenko-accuses-PM-Yulia-Tymoshenko-of-treason.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The employees (not the members) of <a href="/wiki/Oregon" title="Oregon">Oregon</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Oregon_Education_Association" title="Oregon Education Association">largest teachers' union</a> go on strike against the union itself. <a class="external text" href="http://news.opb.org/article/3060-teachers-union-staff-strike-against-teachers-union/" rel="nofollow">(OPB News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Malcolm_Turnbull" title="Malcolm Turnbull">Malcolm Turnbull</a> is elected as the new leader of the Federal <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_Australia" title="Liberal Party of Australia">Liberal Party of Australia</a> and <a href="/wiki/List_of_Australian_Leaders_of_the_Opposition" title="List of Australian Leaders of the Opposition">Leader of the Opposition</a> following a leadership spill. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/story/0,23599,24353392-421,00.html?referrer=email" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Republic_of_China" title="Republic of China">Republic of China</a> adopts <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hanyu_Pinyin" title="Hanyu Pinyin">Hanyu Pinyin</a> as its official <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chinese_romanization" title="Chinese romanization">Chinese romanization</a>, switching from the previously-official <a href="/wiki/Tongyong_Pinyin" title="Tongyong Pinyin">Tongyong Pinyin</a>.<a class="external text" href="http://www.taipeitimes.com/News/taiwan/archives/2008/09/18/2003423528" rel="nofollow">(Taipei Times)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.chinapost.com.tw/taiwan/national/national%20news/2008/09/18/175155/Gov%27t-to.htm" rel="nofollow">(China Post)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_17&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>The emerging <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_baby_milk_scandal" title="2008 baby milk scandal">2008 baby milk scandal</a> shows evidence of coverup by officials during the Olympics. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/26755023/" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">Dow Jones Industrial Average</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Global_stock_market_crash_of_September_2008" title="Global stock market crash of September 2008">falls</a> by 440 points as the bailout of the <a href="/wiki/American_International_Group" title="American International Group">American International Group</a> by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_Reserve" title="Federal Reserve">Federal Reserve</a> fails to reassure jittery investors. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/18/business/18markets.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foreign_Minister_of_Israel" title="Foreign Minister of Israel">Foreign Minister of Israel</a> <a href="/wiki/Tzipi_Livni" title="Tzipi Livni">Tzipi Livni</a> is selected as the new leader of the <a href="/wiki/Kadima" title="Kadima">Kadima</a> party, putting her in position to possibly become the first female <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel" title="Prime Minister of Israel">Prime Minister of Israel</a> since <a href="/wiki/Golda_Meir" title="Golda Meir">Golda Meir</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/worldNews/idUSLH62065120080917" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rwanda" title="Rwanda">Rwanda</a> becomes the first nation where women outnumber men in <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Rwanda" title="Parliament of Rwanda">parliament</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/7620816.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Russian_financial_crisis" title="2008 Russian financial crisis">2008 Russian financial crisis</a>:
<ul>
<li>Trading is suspended for the second day in succession on <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s two main stock exchanges (the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MICEX" title="MICEX">MICEX</a> and the dollar-denominated <a href="/wiki/Russian_Trading_System" title="Russian Trading System">RTS</a>) after shares fall dramatically, forcing the <a href="/wiki/Central_Bank_of_Russia" title="Central Bank of Russia">central bank</a> in <a href="/wiki/Moscow" title="Moscow">Moscow</a> to intervene. <a class="external text" href="http://business.timesonline.co.uk/tol/business/markets/article4772350.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601085&amp;sid=arNaiuHTXLbs&amp;refer=europe" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
<li>Russia's government lends the country's three biggest banks, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sberbank" title="Sberbank">Sberbank</a>, <a href="/wiki/VTB_Bank" title="VTB Bank">VTB Bank</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gazprombank" title="Gazprombank">Gazprombank</a>, as much as 1.13 trillion <a href="/wiki/Ruble" title="Ruble">rubles</a> ($44 billion) for at least three months to boost <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Liquidity" title="Liquidity">liquidity</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601085&amp;sid=a1sZsKZ32kvU&amp;refer=europe" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamic_Jihad_(Yemen)" title="Islamic Jihad (Yemen)">Islamic Jihad</a> claim responsibility for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Yemeni_American_embassy_attack" title="2008 Yemeni American embassy attack">an attack on</a> the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S." title="U.S.">U.S.</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Embassy" title="Embassy">embassy</a> in <a href="/wiki/Yemen" title="Yemen">Yemen</a> that results in 16 confirmed deaths. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/18/world/middleeast/18yemen.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> reports that British bank <a href="/wiki/HBOS" title="HBOS">HBOS</a> is in advanced talks with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lloyds_TSB" title="Lloyds TSB">Lloyds TSB</a> as HBOS share prices plummet as a result of exposure to the <a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">subprime mortgage crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iht.com/articles/ap/2008/09/17/business/EU-Britain-HBOS.php" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>International Herald Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> deploys <a href="/wiki/Sukhoi_Su-30MKI" title="Sukhoi Su-30MKI">Sukhoi Su-30MKI</a> fighter jets capable of carrying <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nuclear_warhead" title="Nuclear warhead">nuclear warheads</a> in <a href="/wiki/Jammu_and_Kashmir" title="Jammu and Kashmir">Jammu and Kashmir</a> amidst continuing <a href="/wiki/Ceasefire" title="Ceasefire">ceasefire</a> violations with <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> along the <a href="/wiki/Line_of_Control" title="Line of Control">Line of Control</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/Fighter_jets_deployed_in_JK_amid_Indo-Pak_tension/articleshow/3493057.cms" rel="nofollow">(<i>Times of India</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Thai_political_crisis" title="2008 Thai political crisis">2008 Thai political crisis</a>: <a href="/wiki/Somchai_Wongsawat" title="Somchai Wongsawat">Somchai Wongsawat</a> has been elected as the next <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Thailand" title="Prime Minister of Thailand">Prime Minister of Thailand</a> by the <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_of_Thailand" title="National Assembly of Thailand">National Assembly of Thailand</a> with King <a href="/wiki/Bhumibol_Adulyadej" title="Bhumibol Adulyadej">Bhumibol Adulyadej</a> having to endorse the selection. <a class="external text" href="http://www.canberratimes.com.au/news/local/news/general/wongsawat-named-as-thailand-pm/1275290.aspx?src=rss" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>The Canberra Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/BAA_Limited" title="BAA Limited">BAA Limited</a> decides to sell <a href="/wiki/Gatwick_Airport" title="Gatwick Airport">Gatwick Airport</a> following a recent ruling by the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> <a href="/wiki/Competition_Commission" title="Competition Commission">Competition Commission</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/business/7620293.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/International_Astronomical_Union" title="International Astronomical Union">International Astronomical Union</a> classifies <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Haumea_(dwarf_planet)" title="Haumea (dwarf planet)">Haumea</a> as the fifth <a href="/wiki/Dwarf_planet" title="Dwarf planet">dwarf planet</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Solar_System" title="Solar System">Solar System</a> and names it after the <a href="/wiki/Haumea_(mythology)" title="Haumea (mythology)">Hawaiian goddess</a> of childbirth and fertility. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iau.org/public_press/news/release/iau0807/" rel="nofollow">(IAU press release)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Papua_New_Guinea" title="Papua New Guinea">Papua New Guinea</a> launches the <a href="/wiki/National_Television_Service" title="National Television Service">National Television Service</a>, a free-to-air state-run channel which competes with <a href="/wiki/EM_TV" title="EM TV">EM TV</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2008/09/17/2367419.htm" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 18, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-18</span>)</span> (Thursday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_18&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_18&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_18&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_South_Ossetia_war" title="2008 South Ossetia war">2008 South Ossetia war</a>:
<ul>
<li>US President <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> will urge <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> to honor its commitment to fully withdraw troops from <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> during his speech at the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">United Nations General Assembly</a> next week, a top White House official said Friday. <a class="external text" href="http://afp.google.com/article/ALeqM5hygXnOmrVbxMVtgYvUOB_AUleCxg" rel="nofollow">(AFP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>Russia says EU observers and extra <a href="/wiki/Organization_for_Security_and_Co-operation_in_Europe" title="Organization for Security and Co-operation in Europe">Organization for Security and Co-operation in Europe</a> (OSCE) monitors should monitor situation on the border land of <a href="/wiki/Georgia_(country)" title="Georgia (country)">Georgia</a> and <a href="/wiki/South_Ossetia" title="South Ossetia">South Ossetia</a> and <a href="/wiki/Abkhazia" title="Abkhazia">Abkhazia</a>. On <a href="/wiki/September_1" title="September 1">September 1</a> Tbilisi has withdrew from Dagomys peace agreement, which was providing legal basis for OSCE monitors in the two states. <a class="external text" href="http://www.eurasianet.org/departments/insight/articles/eav091908.shtml" rel="nofollow">(EurAsia)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Rozi Khan, the Governor of the <a href="/wiki/Chora_District" title="Chora District">Chora District</a> in <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>, is killed in a firefight involving <a href="/wiki/Australian_Army" title="Australian Army">Australian Army</a> soldiers. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2008/09/19/2369166.htm" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sri_Lankan_Civil_War" title="Sri Lankan Civil War">Sri Lankan Civil War</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka_Navy" title="Sri Lanka Navy">Sri Lanka Navy</a> sinks 10 <a href="/wiki/Liberation_Tigers_of_Tamil_Eelam" title="Liberation Tigers of Tamil Eelam">Liberation Tigers of Tamil Eelam</a> (LTTE) boats and kills 25 LTTE rebels in heavy fighting off the port of Nachikkudah in <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka" title="Sri Lanka">Sri Lanka</a>, according to the navy. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iht.com/articles/reuters/2008/09/18/asia/OUKWD-UK-SRILANKA-WAR.php" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>The International Herald Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Russian_financial_crisis" title="2008 Russian financial crisis">2008 Russian financial crisis</a>:
<ul>
<li>Trading is suspended for the third day in succession on <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>'s two main stock exchanges, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MICEX" title="MICEX">MICEX</a> and the dollar-denominated <a href="/wiki/Russian_Trading_System" title="Russian Trading System">RTS</a>, amidst fear of financial collapse. News agencies are quoting Russia's Finance Minister, <a href="/wiki/Alexei_Kudrin" title="Alexei Kudrin">Alexei Kudrin</a>, as saying trading on Russian exchanges won't resume until <a href="/wiki/September_19" title="September 19">September 19</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/news/story/russian-stock-markets-remain-hold/story.aspx?guid=%7B8901F86A-FF6D-4658-BC1C-4D926CA478BF%7D&amp;dist=msr_5" rel="nofollow">(MarketWatch)</a></li>
<li>Officials at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MICEX" title="MICEX">MICEX</a> stock exchange describe conditions in the Russian markets as "extraordinary". <a class="external text" href="http://business.timesonline.co.uk/tol/business/economics/article4780314.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> is facing its worst stock market decline in a decade mainly because of a confidence crisis rather than liquidity problems, Deputy Finance Minister <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Pyotr_Kazakevich&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Pyotr Kazakevich (page does not exist)">Pyotr Kazakevich</a> says. <a class="external text" href="http://www.hurriyet.com.tr/english/finance/9930871.asp?scr=1" rel="nofollow">(Hurriyet)</a></li>
<li>Russian President <a href="/wiki/Dmitry_Medvedev" title="Dmitry Medvedev">Dmitry Medvedev</a> orders ministers to inject another 500 billion <a href="/wiki/Ruble" title="Ruble">rubles</a> (£10.8 billion, US$20 billion) of funds from the state budget into the markets and pledges in remarks broadcast on national television that the financial system would receive "all necessary support". <a class="external text" href="http://business.timesonline.co.uk/tol/business/economics/article4780314.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a>:
<ul>
<li>British bank <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lloyds_TSB" title="Lloyds TSB">Lloyds TSB</a> completes a £12.2bn takeover of rival <a href="/wiki/HBOS" title="HBOS">HBOS</a>, the UK's largest mortgage lender. The <a href="/wiki/Competition_Commission" title="Competition Commission">Competition Commission</a> has allowed the deal as it has government backing, despite the fact that it will leave <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lloyds_TSB" title="Lloyds TSB">Lloyd's HBOS</a> in control of a third of the UK <a href="/wiki/Mortgage_loan" title="Mortgage loan">mortgage</a> market. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/business/7622380.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Swedish_National_Debt_Office" title="Swedish National Debt Office">Swedish National Debt Office</a> announces it is putting a temporary hold on its market commitment in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Treasury_security" title="Treasury security">treasury bills</a> due to the spike in demand for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Treasury_security" title="Treasury security">treasury bonds</a>, which are seen as a safe investment during rocky periods in the financial markets. <a class="external text" href="https://www.riksgalden.se/templates/RGK_Templates/NewsPage____16980.aspx" rel="nofollow">(Riksgäldskontoret)</a></li>
<li>Following the recent rapid fall of the share value of <a href="/wiki/HBOS" title="HBOS">HBOS</a>, The <a href="/wiki/Financial_Services_Authority" title="Financial Services Authority">Financial Services Authority</a> restricts <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Short_selling" title="Short selling">short selling</a> in an attempt to bring about market stability in the <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a>. This action follows a similar move by the <a href="/wiki/U.S._Securities_and_Exchange_Commission" title="U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission">U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission</a> in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> on Wednesday. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/business/7624012.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican</a> presidential candidate <a href="/wiki/John_McCain" title="John McCain">John McCain</a> calls for <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Cox" title="Christopher Cox">Christopher Cox</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chairman" title="Chairman">Chairman</a> of the <a href="/wiki/U.S._Securities_and_Exchange_Commission" title="U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission">U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission</a>, to be dismissed. <a class="external text" href="http://online.wsj.com/article/SB122175692668652881.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Wall Street Journal</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kraft_Foods" title="Kraft Foods">Kraft Foods</a> replaces <a href="/wiki/American_International_Group" title="American International Group">American International Group</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">Dow Jones Industrial Average</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.forbes.com/afxnewslimited/feeds/afx/2008/09/18/afx5441768.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>Forbes</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Securities_and_Exchange_Commission" title="Securities and Exchange Commission">Securities and Exchange Commission</a> declares an emergency ban on <a href="/wiki/Short_(finance)" title="Short (finance)">shorting</a> financial-sector stocks. <a class="external text" href="http://www.msnbc.msn.com/id/26785712" rel="nofollow">(MSNBC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_States_Army" title="United States Army">United States Army</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CH-47_Chinook" title="CH-47 Chinook">CH-47 Chinook</a> helicopter crashes in southern <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a> killing seven <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> soldiers. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/aponline/world/AP-ML-Iraq.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pirate" title="Pirate">Pirates</a> hijack a <a href="/wiki/Greece" title="Greece">Greek</a> <a href="/wiki/Bulk_carrier" title="Bulk carrier">bulk carrier</a> with 25 crew aboard off the coast of <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5ijDA5bgxiHlTvS_r-SSjskS1Tq1wD938UMJO0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a> <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikinews.org/wiki/Somali_pirates_seize_Greek_freighter,_25_crew_in_the_Gulf_of_Aden" title="n:Somali pirates seize Greek freighter, 25 crew in the Gulf of Aden">(Wikinews)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bruessel" title="Bruessel">Bruessel</a>/<a href="/wiki/European_Union" title="European Union">EU</a>:In European media, journalists report that some US politicians and military personnel supported with financial help the Anti-Europe Movement in <a href="/wiki/Ireland" title="Ireland">Ireland</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Lisbon" title="Treaty of Lisbon">Treaty of Lisbon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ftd.de/politik/europa/:Irlands-Nein-Kampagne-USA-sollen-EU-Vertrag-sabotiert-haben/418025.html" rel="nofollow">Ftd:USA sollen EU-Vertrag sabotiert haben</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_19&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_19&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_19&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>Four people die in a plane crash in <a href="/wiki/Columbia,_South_Carolina" title="Columbia, South Carolina">Columbia, South Carolina</a> with <a href="/wiki/Travis_Barker" title="Travis Barker">Travis Barker</a>, formerly of <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Blink_182" title="Blink 182">Blink 182</a>, and <a href="/wiki/DJ_AM" title="DJ AM">DJ AM</a> being critically injured. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/SHOWBIZ/Music/09/20/barker.plane.crash.ap/index.html?section=cnn_latest" rel="nofollow">(AP via CNN)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Financial_crisis_of_2007%E2%80%932010" title="Financial crisis of 2007–2010">Financial crisis of 2007–2010</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/U.S._Securities_and_Exchange_Commission" title="U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission">U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission</a> and <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> <a href="/wiki/Financial_Services_Authority" title="Financial Services Authority">Financial Services Authority</a> take emergency action to temporarily ban <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Short-selling" title="Short-selling">short-selling</a> of financial companies stock. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5j1qYpENSJmaTaTiLWSUFodScpFTwD939NEMG0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_the_Treasury" title="United States Department of the Treasury">United States Department of the Treasury</a> guarantees <a href="/wiki/Money_market" title="Money market">money market</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mutual_funds" title="Mutual funds">mutual funds</a> up to an amount of $50 billion to guarantee their viability. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/20/business/20moneys.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/New_York_Stock_Exchange" title="New York Stock Exchange">New York Stock Exchange</a> responds positively to these initiatives with the <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">Dow Jones Industrial Average</a> rising by 390 points. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/20/business/economy/20cndleadall.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nigerian_Oil_Crisis" title="Nigerian Oil Crisis">Nigerian Oil Crisis</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Movement_for_the_Emancipation_of_the_Niger_Delta" title="Movement for the Emancipation of the Niger Delta">Movement for the Emancipation of the Niger Delta</a> announces that it has blown up a pipeline operated by <a href="/wiki/Royal_Dutch_Shell" title="Royal Dutch Shell">Royal Dutch Shell</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/7624906.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Nigerian oil production has been reduced by 280,000 barrels per day since renewed attacks on oil facilities began. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601116&amp;sid=aAq1GfJZsiME&amp;refer=africa" rel="nofollow">(<i>Bloomberg</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Professor <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Hawking" title="Stephen Hawking">Stephen Hawking</a> unveils the <a href="/wiki/Corpus_Clock" title="Corpus Clock">Corpus Clock</a>, a 'terrifying' new way to read the time, at <a href="/wiki/Corpus_Christi_College,_Cambridge" title="Corpus Christi College, Cambridge">Corpus Christi College, Cambridge</a>, England. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/technology/7625815.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Travis_Barker" title="Travis Barker">Travis Barker</a>, drummer of Pop Punk band <a href="/wiki/Blink-182" title="Blink-182">Blink-182</a> suffers life threatening injuries in a plane crash. <a class="external text" href="http://www.today.com/id/26803108#.Ue1aKW3hdQw" rel="nofollow">(Today.com)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_20&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>A fire in a <a href="/wiki/Nightclub" title="Nightclub">nightclub</a> in the southern <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> city of <a href="/wiki/Shenzhen" title="Shenzhen">Shenzhen</a> results in 43 dead and another 51 injured. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2008/09/21/2370116.htm" rel="nofollow">(AFP via ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li>The Ugandan <a href="/wiki/Lord%27s_Resistance_Army" title="Lord's Resistance Army">Lord's Resistance Army</a> has launched a surprise offensive in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Southern_Sudan" title="Southern Sudan">Southern Sudan</a> hitting an army base and villages in the nearby <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/7625515.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>Residents of <a href="/wiki/Galveston_Island" title="Galveston Island">Galveston Island</a>, <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">Texas</a> are advised that they can return home next Wednesday but there will be little or no services after <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ike_(2008)" title="Hurricane Ike (2008)">Hurricane Ike</a> destroyed much of the town. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/US/09/20/galveston.return/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/George_W._Bush_administration" title="George W. Bush administration">Bush administration</a> asks the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">United States Congress</a> for $700 billion to buy mortgage-related assets to try to resolve the <a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">subprime mortgage crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.usatoday.com/news/washington/2008-09-20-financial-rescue_N.htm?csp=34" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>USA Today</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/War_in_North-West_Pakistan" title="War in North-West Pakistan">War in North-West Pakistan</a>:
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Suicide_bomber" title="Suicide bomber">suicide bomber</a> attacks a <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Army" title="Pakistan Army">Pakistan Army</a> convoy, killing eight soldiers. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20080920-eight-dead-attacks-pakistan-army-convoys" rel="nofollow">(France 24)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Marriott_Hotel_bombing" title="2008 Marriott Hotel bombing">2008 Marriott Hotel bombing</a> occurs. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5jM_dFZu6OlJGY-syTjldIu-BXZeAD93AL9200" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/South_African" title="South African">South African</a> President <a href="/wiki/Thabo_Mbeki" title="Thabo Mbeki">Thabo Mbeki</a> agrees to resign after the ruling <a href="/wiki/African_National_Congress" title="African National Congress">African National Congress</a> requested him to step down.<a class="external text" href="http://africa.reuters.com/top/news/usnBAN051941.html" rel="nofollow">(Reuters Africa via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> detains 13 <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">Indian</a> <a href="/wiki/Fisherman" title="Fisherman">fishermen</a> after they <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Illegal_fishing" title="Illegal fishing">drifted</a> in Pakistani waters. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ptinews.com/pti\ptisite.nsf/0/88B45F6EB3586711652574CA003A5ACF?OpenDocument" rel="nofollow">(Press Trust of India)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Cartoon_Network" title="Cartoon Network">Cartoon Network</a>'s hit <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Action_(fiction)" title="Action (fiction)">action</a>-<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Animated" title="Animated">animated</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Programming_block" title="Programming block">programming block</a> <a href="/wiki/Toonami" title="Toonami">Toonami</a> went completely <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Off_the_air" title="Off the air">off the air</a>.</li>
</ul>
