<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><i><a href="/wiki/Mad_Men" title="Mad Men">Mad Men</a></i> wins the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Emmy_Awards" title="Emmy Awards">Emmy Award</a> for Best Drama and <i><a href="/wiki/30_Rock" title="30 Rock">30 Rock</a></i> wins for Best Comedy at the <a href="/wiki/60th_Primetime_Emmy_Awards" title="60th Primetime Emmy Awards">60th Primetime Emmy Awards</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/marketsNews/idUSN2152372920080922" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Goldman_Sachs" title="Goldman Sachs">Goldman Sachs</a> and <a href="/wiki/Morgan_Stanley" title="Morgan Stanley">Morgan Stanley</a>, the two last remaining independent <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Investment_bank" title="Investment bank">investment banks</a> on <a href="/wiki/Wall_Street" title="Wall Street">Wall Street</a>, become bank holding companies as a result of the <a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">subprime mortgage crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://dealbook.blogs.nytimes.com/2008/09/21/goldman-morgan-to-become-bank-holding-companies/index.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>The number of babies in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> hospitalized due to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_baby_milk_scandal" title="2008 baby milk scandal">adulterated milk products and infant formula</a> reaches 12,892. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/asiapcf/09/21/china.tainted.milk/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Social_Democrats_(Slovenia)" title="Social Democrats (Slovenia)">Social Democrats</a>, led by <a href="/wiki/Borut_Pahor" title="Borut Pahor">Borut Pahor</a>, presumably win the <a href="/wiki/Slovenia" title="Slovenia">Slovenian</a> <a href="/wiki/Slovenian_parliamentary_election,_2008" title="Slovenian parliamentary election, 2008">parliamentary election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/heraldsun/story/0,21985,24382710-663,00.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>Melbourne Herald Sun</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> wins the <a href="/wiki/2008_Ryder_Cup" title="2008 Ryder Cup">Ryder Cup</a> for the first time since <a href="/wiki/1999_Ryder_Cup" title="1999 Ryder Cup">1999</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.timesonline.co.uk/tol/sport/golf/article4799673.ece" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Times</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel" title="Prime Minister of Israel">Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Ehud_Olmert" title="Ehud Olmert">Ehud Olmert</a> officially submits his resignation to <a href="/wiki/President_of_Israel" title="President of Israel">President</a> <a href="/wiki/Shimon_Peres" title="Shimon Peres">Shimon Peres</a>. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foreign_Affairs_Minister_of_Israel" title="Foreign Affairs Minister of Israel">Foreign Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Tzipi_Livni" title="Tzipi Livni">Tzipi Livni</a> begins talks on forming a new government. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5hcX49mNGhMPjANq3C-wSH833a0swD93B81B80" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tyrone_GAA" title="Tyrone GAA">Tyrone</a> beat <a href="/wiki/Kerry_GAA" title="Kerry GAA">Kerry</a> 1-15 to 0-14 to win the <a href="/wiki/All-Ireland_Senior_Football_Championship" title="All-Ireland Senior Football Championship">All-Ireland Senior Football Championship</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/All-Ireland_Senior_Football_Championship_2008" title="All-Ireland Senior Football Championship 2008">2008</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/sport/gaa/championship/2008/0921/tyrone_kerry.html?gaa" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_New_York_Yankees" title="The New York Yankees">The New York Yankees</a> beat The <a href="/wiki/Baltimore_Orioles" title="Baltimore Orioles">Baltimore Orioles</a>, 7-3, at their last home game at <a href="/wiki/Yankee_Stadium_(1923)" title="Yankee Stadium (1923)">Yankee Stadium</a>. This is the last time the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Yankees" title="New York Yankees">New York Yankees</a> play at <a href="/wiki/Yankee_Stadium_(1923)" title="Yankee Stadium (1923)">Yankee Stadium</a> before moving to the <a href="/wiki/Yankee_Stadium" title="Yankee Stadium">New Yankee Stadium</a> across the street. <a class="external text" href="http://newyork.yankees.mlb.com/news/wrap.jsp?ymd=20080921&amp;content_id=3525626&amp;vkey=wrapup2005&amp;fext=.jsp&amp;team=home&amp;c_id=nyy" rel="nofollow">(Yankees.com)</a></li>
</ul>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Herman_Simm" title="Herman Simm">Herman Simm</a>, a former head of security at the <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonian</a> Defense Ministry, and his wife <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Heete_Simm" title="Heete Simm">Heete Simm</a>, who works as a lawyer at <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>'s National Police Board, are arrested on suspicion of spying for <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iht.com/articles/ap/2008/09/22/europe/EU-Estonia-Spy-Suspects.php" rel="nofollow">(<i>The International Herald Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li>Four people die in <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a> as a result of heavy rains. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/story/0,2933,426163,00.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/South_Africa" title="South Africa">South Africa</a>'s ruling <a href="/wiki/African_National_Congress" title="African National Congress">African National Congress</a> party names deputy president <a href="/wiki/Kgalema_Motlanthe" title="Kgalema Motlanthe">Kgalema Motlanthe</a> as the successor to President <a href="/wiki/Thabo_Mbeki" title="Thabo Mbeki">Thabo Mbeki</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601116&amp;sid=anGwLoz3em0o&amp;refer=africa" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg News)</a></li>
<li>More than 18,000 archived radio programs are indefinitely lost after the main <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Computer_server" title="Computer server">computer server</a> at <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sveriges_Radio" title="Sveriges Radio">National Radio</a> crashed last month. <a class="external text" href="http://www.resume.se/nyheter/2008/09/22/serverkrasch-pa-sr-18-000-/" rel="nofollow">(Resume)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democratic_Party_(Japan)_leadership_election,_2008" title="Liberal Democratic Party (Japan) leadership election, 2008">Liberal Democratic Party (Japan) leadership election, 2008</a>: <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>'s ruling <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democratic_Party_(Japan)" title="Liberal Democratic Party (Japan)">Liberal Democratic Party</a> chooses former <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foreign_Minister_of_Japan" title="Foreign Minister of Japan">Foreign Minister of Japan</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taro_Aso" title="Taro Aso">Taro Aso</a> as the next <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Prime Minister of Japan</a> replacing <a href="/wiki/Yasuo_Fukuda" title="Yasuo Fukuda">Yasuo Fukuda</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.afp.com/english/news/stories/newsmlmmd.f211f178f3200b11cc14baa44acfe7bf.271.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Edward_Natapei" title="Edward Natapei">Edward Natapei</a> is elected the new <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Vanuatu" title="Prime Minister of Vanuatu">Prime Minister</a> of <a href="/wiki/Vanuatu" title="Vanuatu">Vanuatu</a> following the <a href="/wiki/Vanuatuan_general_election,_2008" title="Vanuatuan general election, 2008">2008 general elections</a> replacing <a href="/wiki/Ham_Lini" title="Ham Lini">Ham Lini</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.iht.com/articles/ap/2008/09/22/asia/AS-Vanuatu-Politics.php" rel="nofollow">(<i>The International Herald Tribune</i>)</a></li>
<li>15 people, including 11 foreign nationals, are kidnapped near <a href="/wiki/Aswan" title="Aswan">Aswan</a> in southern <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/middle_east/7629171.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Radiocarbon_dating" title="Radiocarbon dating">Radiocarbon dating</a> estimates that <a href="/wiki/Stonehenge" title="Stonehenge">Stonehenge</a> was constructed around 2300 BC. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/sci/tech/7625145.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Emergency_Economic_Stabilization_Act_of_2008" title="Emergency Economic Stabilization Act of 2008">Emergency Economic Stabilization Act of 2008</a> is debated on by the <a href="/wiki/110th_United_States_Congress" title="110th United States Congress">110th United States Congress</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/22/business/22paulson.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">Dow Jones Industrial Average</a> falls by 370 points due to uncertainty over the plan. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/23/business/23markets.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A car is driven into a group of people in <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a> in what <a href="/wiki/Israel" title="Israel">Israeli</a> authorities are describing as a "terror attack". <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/world/middle_east/7630534.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_23&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_23&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pakistani_people" title="Pakistani people">Pakistani</a> soldiers and tribesmen reportedly shoot down a suspected U.S. military drone near the village of Jalal Khel in <a href="/wiki/South_Waziristan" title="South Waziristan">South Waziristan</a>. The report comes a day after intelligence officers said two <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Helicopters" title="Helicopters">helicopters</a> crossed a mile into Pakistan over <a href="/wiki/North_Waziristan" title="North Waziristan">North Waziristan</a>, but flew off after Pakistani troops and tribesmen opened fire. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5hkiMxbHNH0BqgpWA2ZG6VD6wVTmAD93CN8T01" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>Government officials say that the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation" title="Federal Bureau of Investigation">Federal Bureau of Investigation</a> is looking into possible <a href="/wiki/Fraud" title="Fraud">fraud</a> for mortgage financing companies <a href="/wiki/Fannie_Mae" title="Fannie Mae">Fannie Mae</a> and <a href="/wiki/Freddie_Mac" title="Freddie Mac">Freddie Mac</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lehman_Brothers" title="Lehman Brothers">Lehman Brothers</a>, and insurer <a href="/wiki/American_International_Group" title="American International Group">American International Group</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://money.cnn.com/2008/09/23/news/companies/fbi_finance.ap/index.htm" rel="nofollow">(AP via CNNMoney)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Large_Hadron_Collider" title="Large Hadron Collider">Large Hadron Collider</a> near <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a> is shut down until the northern <a href="/wiki/Spring_(season)" title="Spring (season)">spring</a> while engineers probe magnet failures. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/science/nature/7632408.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ben_Bernanke" title="Ben Bernanke">Ben Bernanke</a>, the Chairman of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_Reserve" title="Federal Reserve">Federal Reserve</a>, warns the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">United States Congress</a> that failure to pass the <a href="/wiki/Emergency_Economic_Stabilization_Act_of_2008" title="Emergency Economic Stabilization Act of 2008">Emergency Economic Stabilization Act of 2008</a> quickly would make a <a href="/wiki/Recession" title="Recession">recession</a> more likely. <a class="external text" href="http://www.miamiherald.com/news/politics/campaign-2008/story/697366.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Miami Herald</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japanese</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Investment_bank" title="Investment bank">investment bank</a> <a href="/wiki/Nomura_Holdings" title="Nomura Holdings">Nomura Holdings</a> acquires the <a href="/wiki/Europe" title="Europe">European</a>, <a href="/wiki/Asia" title="Asia">Asian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Middle_East" title="Middle East">Middle Eastern</a> equities and investment banking operations of <a href="/wiki/Lehman_Brothers" title="Lehman Brothers">Lehman Brothers</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/news/story/nomura-acquires-european-operations-lehman/story.aspx?guid=%7B3F8882D9%2DD10C%2D4406%2D8979%2D701FA1BB8BD6%7D&amp;dist=hplatest" rel="nofollow">(MarketWatch)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Sveriges_Television" title="Sveriges Television">National Television</a> issues a public apology for a "misleading" report on comments made by foreign minister <a href="/wiki/Carl_Bildt" title="Carl Bildt">Carl Bildt</a> about Sweden's intelligence services. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thelocal.se/14506/20080923/" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Local</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Colin_Barnett" title="Colin Barnett">Colin Barnett</a> is sworn in as the 29th <a href="/wiki/Premier_of_Western_Australia" title="Premier of Western Australia">Premier</a> of <a href="/wiki/Western_Australia" title="Western Australia">Western Australia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thewest.com.au/default.aspx?MenuID=77&amp;ContentID=99212" rel="nofollow">(<i>The West Australian</i>)</a></li>
<li>Eleven die in a <a href="/wiki/Kauhajoki_school_shooting" title="Kauhajoki school shooting">school shooting</a> in <a href="/wiki/Kauhajoki" title="Kauhajoki">Kauhajoki</a>, <a href="/wiki/Finland" title="Finland">Finland</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/in_depth/7630969.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_24&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_24&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_24&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>At least 17 civilians are killed in battles between <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Islamist" title="Islamist">Islamist</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Insurgent" title="Insurgent">militants</a> and <a href="/wiki/African_Union" title="African Union">African Union</a> peacekeepers in the <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somali</a> capital <a href="/wiki/Mogadishu" title="Mogadishu">Mogadishu</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/africa/09/24/somalia.fighting/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> <a href="/wiki/George_W._Bush" title="George W. Bush">George W. Bush</a> <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/President_Bush%27s_remarks_to_the_nation_re_the_Wall_Street_crisis,_24_September_2008" title="wikisource:President Bush's remarks to the nation re the Wall Street crisis, 24 September 2008">addresses the nation on prime time television</a> to discuss the crisis and the <a href="/wiki/Emergency_Economic_Stabilization_Act_of_2008" title="Emergency Economic Stabilization Act of 2008">Paulson plan</a>. He warns that the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> faces a "long and painful recession" if the package is not passed. <a class="external text" href="http://www.sfgate.com/cgi-bin/article.cgi?f=/n/a/2008/09/24/national/w181606D88.DTL&amp;feed=rss.news" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>San Francisco Chronicle</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://canadianpress.google.com/article/ALeqM5gMENce1TaDLlbhO1EVASVcuj3fAw" rel="nofollow">(Canadian Press via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_of_the_United_States" title="Senate of the United States">Senator</a> <a href="/wiki/John_McCain" title="John McCain">John McCain</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">Republican Party</a> nominee in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2008" title="United States presidential election, 2008">presidential election</a>, postpones campaigning and seeks deferral of a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_debates,_2008#Proposed_postponement" title="United States presidential election debates, 2008">presidential debate</a> so that he can return to <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington_D.C." title="Washington D.C.">Washington D.C.</a> to discuss the <a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">subprime mortgage crisis</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Emergency_Economic_Stabilization_Act_of_2008" title="Emergency Economic Stabilization Act of 2008">Paulson Plan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/25/us/politics/25mccain.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>President Bush invites Senator McCain, Senator <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Party_(United_States)" title="Democratic Party (United States)">Democratic Party</a> and leaders of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">United States Congress</a> to a meeting at the <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">White House</a> tomorrow to discuss the crisis. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nysun.com/national/bush-invites-mccain-obama-to-white-house/86543/" rel="nofollow">(AP via the <i>New York Sun</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Preliminary findings made for the <a href="/wiki/American_Geophysical_Union" title="American Geophysical Union">American Geophysical Union</a> that support the <a href="/wiki/Clathrate_gun_hypothesis" title="Clathrate gun hypothesis">Clathrate gun hypothesis</a>, indicate the possible release of millions of tons of <a href="/wiki/Methane" title="Methane">methane</a>, a <a href="/wiki/Greenhouse_gas" title="Greenhouse gas">greenhouse gas</a>, from <a href="/wiki/Arctic" title="Arctic">Arctic</a> <a href="/wiki/Seabed" title="Seabed">seabeds</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.independent.co.uk/environment/climate-change/exclusive-the-methane-time-bomb-938932.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Independent</i>)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Diet_of_Japan" title="Diet of Japan">Diet</a> elects <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Taro_Aso" title="Taro Aso">Taro Aso</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Liberal_Democratic_Party_(Japan)" title="Liberal Democratic Party (Japan)">Liberal Democratic Party</a> as the new <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Japan" title="Prime Minister of Japan">Prime Minister of Japan</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/asiapcf/09/23/japan.politics.ap/index.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via CNN)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.afp.com/english/news/stories/newsmlmmd.9ecb3d3491dae15c197fc6edb44cf938.711.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Tomislav_Nikoli%C4%87" title="Tomislav Nikolić">Tomislav Nikolić</a> announces that his party (a splinter from the <a href="/wiki/Serbian_Radical_Party" title="Serbian Radical Party">Serbian Radical Party</a>) will be called <a href="/wiki/Serbian_Progressive_Party" title="Serbian Progressive Party">Serbian Progressive Party</a> and that it will be founded on 21 October 2008. <a class="external text" href="http://www.b92.net/eng/news/politics-article.php?yyyy=2008&amp;mm=09&amp;dd=24&amp;nav_id=53724" rel="nofollow">(B92)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Hagupit_(2008)" title="Typhoon Hagupit (2008)">Typhoon Hagupit</a> hits <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> and southern <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">China</a>, killing at least eight. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/7632949.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 25, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-25</span>)</span> (Thursday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_25&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_25&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_25&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistani</a> and <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> forces <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tanai_border_repel" title="Tanai border repel">exchange fire</a> on the Afghan-Pakistan border. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/26/world/asia/26military.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Senior members of the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">United States Congress</a> agree on a legislative deal to <a href="/wiki/Emergency_Economic_Stabilization_Act_of_2008" title="Emergency Economic Stabilization Act of 2008">bail out the U.S. financial system</a> from lingering effects of the <a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">subprime mortgage crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/story/0,23599,24405024-2,00.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via News Limited)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Texas_Supreme_Court" title="Texas Supreme Court">Texas Supreme Court</a> denies a petition by the <a href="/wiki/Bob_Barr" title="Bob Barr">Bob Barr</a> US Presidential campaign seeking removal of Senators <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_McCain" title="John McCain">John McCain</a> from that state's ballot due to both candidates missing the filing deadline. <a class="external text" href="http://www.supreme.courts.state.tx.us/Historical/2008/sep/092308.htm" rel="nofollow">(TX Supreme Court)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nolanchart.com/article4987.html" rel="nofollow">(Nolan Report)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.dallasnews.com/sharedcontent/APStories/stories/D93CLMO82.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>Dallas Morning News</i>)</a></li>
<li>An effigy of <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> is found hanging from a tree at <a href="/wiki/George_Fox_University" title="George Fox University">George Fox University</a> in <a href="/wiki/Newberg,_Oregon" title="Newberg, Oregon">Newberg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Oregon" title="Oregon">Oregon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5hlnR7kQP7tXQKA0872BAweYKqPFQD93DPDBG0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>A young <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canadian</a> man is found guilty in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2006_Toronto_terrorism_case" title="2006 Toronto terrorism case">2006 Toronto terrorism case</a> of participating in a plot to storm the <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_Canada" title="Parliament of Canada">Parliament of Canada</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Behead" title="Behead">behead</a> the <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Canada" title="Prime Minister of Canada">Prime Minister of Canada</a>, <a href="/wiki/Stephen_Harper" title="Stephen Harper">Stephen Harper</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/americas/09/25/canada.plot.ap/index.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via CNN)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_economy" title="United States economy">United States economy</a>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jobless" title="Jobless">Jobless</a> claims in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> rise to a seven-year high while orders for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Durable_goods" title="Durable goods">durable goods</a> fall to their lowest level in 18 months, underscoring the weakness of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_economy" title="United States economy">United States economy</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxbusiness.com/story/markets/economy/durable-good-jobless-claims-numbers-underscore-dour-economy/" rel="nofollow">(Fox Business)</a></li>
<li>Home sales in the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> during <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/August_2008" title="August 2008">August 2008</a> fall to a 17-year low. <a class="external text" href="http://www.bloomberg.com/apps/news?pid=20601206&amp;sid=a_zAnYoBrQsg" rel="nofollow">(Bloomberg)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Following the purchase of <a href="/wiki/British_Energy" title="British Energy">British Energy</a> by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Electricit%C3%A9_de_France" title="Electricité de France">Electricité de France</a>, plans for a new <a href="/wiki/Hinkley_Point_C_nuclear_power_station" title="Hinkley Point C nuclear power station">Hinkley Point C nuclear power station</a> have been announced. <a class="external text" href="http://www.world-nuclear-news.org/NN_New_dawn_for_UK_nuclear_power_2409081.html" rel="nofollow">(Nuclear News)</a></li>
<li>The death toll from <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Hagupit_(2008)" title="Typhoon Hagupit (2008)">Typhoon Hagupit</a> rises to 18 with 10 people dead in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">People's Republic of China</a> as well as 8 people killed earlier in the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/weather/09/25/china.typhoon/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Kgalema_Motlanthe" title="Kgalema Motlanthe">Kgalema Motlanthe</a> is sworn in as the third post-<a href="/wiki/Apartheid" title="Apartheid">apartheid</a> <a href="/wiki/President_of_South_Africa" title="President of South Africa">President of South Africa</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.afp.com/english/news/stories/newsmlmmd.f05a6c56658cfd31cf9eed3bf8163054.131.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Dark_flow" title="Dark flow">Dark flow</a>, a new and unexplained cosmic phenomenon, is observed by <a href="/wiki/Astronomy" title="Astronomy">astronomers</a> for the first time. <a class="external text" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/earth/main.jhtml?view=DETAILS&amp;grid=&amp;xml=/earth/2008/09/24/scispace124.xml" rel="nofollow">(<i>The Daily Telegraph</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Shenzhou_7" title="Shenzhou 7">Shenzhou 7</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Shenzhou_program" title="Shenzhou program">third</a> manned <a href="/wiki/Chinese_space_program" title="Chinese space program">Chinese spaceflight</a>, is successfully launched with three crew members, with a planned first Chinese <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spacewalk" title="Spacewalk">spacewalk</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://xinhua.cn" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a><a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/26/world/asia/26space.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_26&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>

<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Senate_of_the_United_States" title="Senate of the United States">Senators</a> <a href="/wiki/John_McCain" title="John McCain">John McCain</a> and <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">Barack Obama</a> take part in the first of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election_debates,_2008" title="United States presidential election debates, 2008">United States presidential election debates</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2008/09/27/2375920.htm?WT.mc_id=newsmail" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Chinese_Milk_Scandal" title="2008 Chinese Milk Scandal">2008 Chinese Milk Scandal</a>: <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> detect <a href="/wiki/Melamine" title="Melamine">melamine</a> in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> food products including <a href="/wiki/Breakfast_cereal" title="Breakfast cereal">breakfast cereals</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cracker_(food)" title="Cracker (food)">crackers</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.chron.com/disp/story.mpl/chronicle/6024432.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Houston Chronicle</i>)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Germany" title="Germany">German</a> <a href="/wiki/Commando" title="Commando">commandos</a> storm a <a href="/wiki/KLM" title="KLM">KLM</a> <a href="/wiki/Airliner" title="Airliner">airliner</a> at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cologne-Bonn_Airport" title="Cologne-Bonn Airport">Cologne-Bonn Airport</a> and arrest two men suspected of planning to carry out a <a href="/wiki/Terrorism" title="Terrorism">terrorist</a> attack. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/story/0,23599,24407042-2,00.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP via News Limited)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a>:
<ul>
<li>In the biggest bank failure in American history, the <a href="/wiki/Federal_Deposit_Insurance_Corporation" title="Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation">Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation</a> seizes <a href="/wiki/Washington_Mutual" title="Washington Mutual">Washington Mutual</a> and sells most of the bank to <a href="/wiki/JPMorgan_Chase" title="JPMorgan Chase">JPMorgan Chase</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/26/business/26wamu.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.fdic.gov/news/news/press/2008/pr08085.html" rel="nofollow">(FDIC)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A Ukrainian vessel carrying 30 <a href="/wiki/T-72" title="T-72">T-72</a> tanks is captured by pirates 200 miles off <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalian</a> coast. <a href="/wiki/Russia" title="Russia">Russia</a> sends its military ship to combat <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Piracy_in_Somalia" title="Piracy in Somalia">piracy in Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/27/world/africa/27pirates.html" rel="nofollow">(<i>The New York Times</i>)</a></li>
</ul>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 27, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-27</span>)</span> (Saturday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_27&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_27&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/27_September_2008_Delhi_blast" title="27 September 2008 Delhi blast">bomb blast</a> in <a href="/wiki/Delhi" title="Delhi">Delhi</a>, <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a> kills 2 and injures 23. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/Blast_in_Mehrauli_area_in_Delhi_2_killed/articleshow/3534219.cms" rel="nofollow">(TOI)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2008 Atlantic hurricane season">2008 Atlantic hurricane season</a>: Tropical Storm Kyle strengthens into <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Kyle_(2008)" title="Hurricane Kyle (2008)">Hurricane Kyle</a> with predictions that it will make landfall in the <a href="/wiki/New_England" title="New England">New England</a> region of the <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> or <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>'s <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maritime_Provinces" title="Maritime Provinces">Maritime Provinces</a> on Sunday. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/newsOne/idUSTRE48Q37Z20080927" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> passes a large spending bill including $25 billion in taxpayer subsidised loans for <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Automaker" title="Automaker">automakers</a> and the end of <a href="/wiki/Offshore_drilling" title="Offshore drilling">offshore drilling</a> bans. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5injFfO8MlwJfFFF_n29IR630N94AD93F7NSG0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/People%27s_Council_of_Turkmenistan" title="People's Council of Turkmenistan">People's Council</a> of <a href="/wiki/Turkmenistan" title="Turkmenistan">Turkmenistan</a>, implementing changes approved in the <a href="/wiki/Constitution_of_Turkmenistan" title="Constitution of Turkmenistan">Constitution</a>, passes a vote to abolish itself and allow opposition parties. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/7638102.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>During mission <a href="/wiki/Shenzhou_7" title="Shenzhou 7">Shenzhou 7</a>, <a href="/wiki/Zhai_Zhigang" title="Zhai Zhigang">Zhai Zhigang</a> successfully performs the first spacewalk by a Chinese <a href="/wiki/Astronaut" title="Astronaut">astronaut</a>, as <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">China</a> becomes the third country to carry out <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra-vehicular_activity" title="Extra-vehicular activity">extra-vehicular activity</a> independently. <a class="external text" href="http://scitech.blogs.cnn.com/" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>In Australian football, the <a href="/wiki/Hawthorn_Football_Club" title="Hawthorn Football Club">Hawthorn Football Club</a> defeats the <a href="/wiki/Geelong_Football_Club" title="Geelong Football Club">Geelong Football Club</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2008_AFL_Grand_Final" title="2008 AFL Grand Final">2008 AFL Grand Final</a> by 115 points to 89. <a class="external text" href="http://www.abc.net.au/news/stories/2008/09/27/2375997.htm" rel="nofollow">(ABC News Australia)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Damascus_car_bomb" title="2008 Damascus car bomb">2008 Damascus car bomb</a>: A suspected <a href="/wiki/Car_bomb" title="Car bomb">car bomb</a> targeting a military installation in <a href="/wiki/Damascus" title="Damascus">Damascus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a> kills at least 17 and injures 14 others. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/middle_east/7639137.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>A 12.9 million digit <a href="/wiki/Mersenne_prime" title="Mersenne prime">Mersenne prime</a> is discovered. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5jep9BkLvN3HAjMV3Z42B78HLCJdwD93F5DT01" rel="nofollow">(AP via <i>Los Angeles Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>Government officials announce plans to nationalise British bank <a href="/wiki/Bradford_%26_Bingley" title="Bradford &amp; Bingley">Bradford &amp; Bingley</a> in the aftermath of the <a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">subprime mortgage crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/business/7640143.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">United Nations Security Council</a> passed <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_resolution" title="United Nations Security Council resolution">Resolution</a> 1835 on <a href="/wiki/Iran" title="Iran">Iran</a>, calling for compliance with previous resolutions, with no further sanctions. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/in_depth/7640133.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 28, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-28</span>)</span> (Sunday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_28&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_28&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_28&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>

<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/SpaceX" title="SpaceX">SpaceX</a> <a href="/wiki/Falcon_1" title="Falcon 1">Falcon 1</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Falcon_1_Flight_4" title="Falcon 1 Flight 4">makes orbit</a>, becoming the first privately developed liquid-fueled <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Space_launch_vehicle" title="Space launch vehicle">space launch vehicle</a> to do so. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5iF-6npNsKa0n_7aLm8tJvuHWt4JgD93G1LC00" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a>:
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_Congress" title="United States Congress">US Congressional</a> leaders and the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/George_W._Bush_administration" title="George W. Bush administration">George W. Bush administration</a> reach an outline <a href="/wiki/Emergency_Economic_Stabilization_Act_of_2008" title="Emergency Economic Stabilization Act of 2008">Emergency Economic Stabilization Act of 2008</a> of a bailout of financial institutions as a result of the <a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">subprime mortgage crisis</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/newsOne/idUSTRE48R0BP20080928" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">British</a> bank <a href="/wiki/Bradford_%26_Bingley" title="Bradford &amp; Bingley">Bradford &amp; Bingley</a> is to be purchased by the <a href="/wiki/HM_Treasury" title="HM Treasury">Treasury</a> and <a href="/wiki/Financial_Services_Authority" title="Financial Services Authority">Financial Services Authority</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/business/7640143.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Belgium" title="Belgium">Belgian</a> bank <a href="/wiki/Fortis_(finance)" title="Fortis (finance)">Fortis</a> NV is partly nationalised as part of an 11.4 billion <a href="/wiki/Euro" title="Euro">euro</a> rescue package funded by the Governments of <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Netherlands</a>, Belgium and <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg" title="Luxembourg">Luxembourg</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://ap.google.com/article/ALeqM5gq42vLUmcA9LTFzCEF-EN1vnhV8wD93G2A0G0" rel="nofollow">(AP via Google News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Piracy_in_Somalia" title="Piracy in Somalia">Piracy in Somalia</a>:
<ul>
<li>The captain of a Ukrainian vessel (<a href="/wiki/MV_Faina" title="MV Faina">MV Faina</a>) loaded with tanks and weapons that was seized off the African coast says one crew member has died. <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/africa/09/28/somalia.piracy.ukraine/index.html" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a></li>
<li>Somali pirates were surrounded by several foreign warships off the central coast of <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.france24.com/en/20080928-foreign-warships-surround-somali-pirates-somalia&amp;navi=AFRIQUE" rel="nofollow">(France 24)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/People%27s_Republic_of_China" title="People's Republic of China">Chinese</a> <a href="/wiki/Astronaut" title="Astronaut">astronauts</a> return safely as the <a href="/wiki/Shenzhou_7" title="Shenzhou 7">Shenzhou 7</a> re-entry capsule lands. This marks the third country to successfully return three astronauts from space, and the third country to successfully return a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spacewalk" title="Spacewalk">spacewalker</a> from space. And the mission marks the third country to successfully develop and deploy a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Spacesuit" title="Spacesuit">spacesuit</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://xinhua.cn" rel="nofollow">(Xinhua)</a></li>
<li>Four days after the formation of new <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a> <a href="/wiki/Cabinet_(government)" title="Cabinet (government)">cabinet</a>, Transport Minister <a href="/wiki/Nariaki_Nakayama" title="Nariaki Nakayama">Nariaki Nakayama</a> resigns after series of controversial speeches. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/7640197.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Haile_Gebrselassie" title="Haile Gebrselassie">Haile Gebrselassie</a> of <a href="/wiki/Ethiopia" title="Ethiopia">Ethiopia</a> sets a new world record in the <a href="/wiki/Marathon" title="Marathon">marathon</a> of two hours three minutes 58 seconds at the <a href="/wiki/Berlin_Marathon" title="Berlin Marathon">Berlin Marathon</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/sportsNews/idUSTRE48R10820080928?feedType=RSS&amp;feedName=sportsNews" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Elections
<ul>
<li>In the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bavaria_state_election,_2008" title="Bavaria state election, 2008">Bavaria state election, 2008</a>, the rightist <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Christian_Social_Union_of_Bavaria" title="Christian Social Union of Bavaria">CSU</a> loses its absolute majority after 40 years. <a class="external text" href="http://www.dw-world.de/dw/article/0,2144,3676808,00.html" rel="nofollow">(Deutsche Welle)</a></li>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Belarus" title="Belarus">Belarus</a> go to the polls for the <a href="/wiki/Belarusian_parliamentary_election,_2008" title="Belarusian parliamentary election, 2008">Belarusian parliamentary elections</a>. According to election officials, allies of <a href="/wiki/President_of_Belarus" title="President of Belarus">President of Belarus</a> <a href="/wiki/Alexander_Lukashenko" title="Alexander Lukashenko">Alexander Lukashenko</a> will win all 110 seats renewing concerns about the process.<a class="external text" href="http://www.theglobeandmail.com/servlet/story/RTGAM.20080927.wbelarus0927/BNStory/International/home" rel="nofollow">(Reuters via <i>The Globe and Mail</i>)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://voanews.com/english/2008-09-29-voa4.cfm" rel="nofollow">(Voice of America)</a></li>
<li>Voters in <a href="/wiki/Austria" title="Austria">Austria</a> go to the polls for the <a href="/wiki/Austrian_legislative_election,_2008" title="Austrian legislative election, 2008">Austrian legislative election</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.afp.com/english/news/stories/newsmlmmd.49a009e41d6df1ad48bec810cd48a5cc.2e1.html" rel="nofollow">(AFP)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Fernando_Alonso" title="Fernando Alonso">Fernando Alonso</a> <a href="/wiki/2008_Singapore_Grand_Prix" title="2008 Singapore Grand Prix">wins</a> the <a href="/wiki/Singapore" title="Singapore">Singapore</a> <a href="/wiki/Singapore_Grand_Prix" title="Singapore Grand Prix">Grand Prix</a> in <a href="/wiki/Formula_One" title="Formula One">Formula One</a>'s first night race. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/sport1/hi/motorsport/formula_one/7640668.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>

<tr>
<td>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 29, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-29</span>)</span> (Monday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_29&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_29&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_29&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/29_September_2008_western_India_bombings" title="29 September 2008 western India bombings">Three bombs</a> go off in <a href="/wiki/Western_India" title="Western India">western India</a>, killing 8 people and injuring 30. <a class="external text" href="http://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/Blasts_in_Maharashtra_Gujarat_8_killed/articleshow/3542011.cms" rel="nofollow">(TOI)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/United_States_Attorney_General" title="United States Attorney General">United States Attorney General</a> <a href="/wiki/Michael_Mukasey" title="Michael Mukasey">Michael Mukasey</a> announces the appointment of a <a href="/wiki/Special_prosecutor" title="Special prosecutor">special prosecutor</a> to investigate the <a href="/wiki/Dismissal_of_U.S._attorneys_controversy" title="Dismissal of U.S. attorneys controversy">firings</a> of nine <a href="/wiki/United_States_Attorney" title="United States Attorney">U.S. attorneys</a> in 2006. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cnn.com/2008/POLITICS/09/29/us.attorneys/index.html?eref=rss_politics" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a>:
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._House_of_Representatives" title="U.S. House of Representatives">House of Representatives</a> rejects a <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Proposed_bailout_of_U.S._financial_system_(2008)" title="Proposed bailout of U.S. financial system (2008)">proposed bailout of the U.S. financial system</a>.<a class="external text" href="http://news.yahoo.com/s/ap/20080929/ap_on_bi_ge/financial_meltdown" rel="nofollow">(Associated Press)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/09/30/business/30bailout.html" rel="nofollow">(New York Times)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/News/Story/Story.aspx?guid=%7B4A947999%2DA373%2D47A9%2DBF29%2DEB8C65CC68C4%7D&amp;siteid=mktw" rel="nofollow">(MarketWatch)</a></li>
<li>Head of the <a href="/wiki/Swedish_National_Debt_Office" title="Swedish National Debt Office">Swedish National Debt Office</a> <a href="/wiki/Bo_Lundgren" title="Bo Lundgren">Bo Lundgren</a> says that the $700 billion U.S. financial industry bailout is based on too-optimistic valuations, and may not be enough to restore confidence in the financial system. <a class="external text" href="http://di.se/Avdelningar/Artikel.aspx?stat=0&amp;ArticleID=2008%5c09%5c29%5c303234&amp;SectionId=Ettan&amp;menusection=Startsidan;Huvudnyheter" rel="nofollow">(Dagens industri)</a></li>
<li>The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/German_government" title="German government">German government</a> and private banks inject 35 billion Euros into the struggling <a href="/wiki/Hypo_Real_Estate" title="Hypo Real Estate">Hypo Real Estate</a>, a bank that is heavily involved in the real estate business. The bank had been struggling because its Irish subsidy Depfa Bank had suffered massive losses during the subprime mortgage crisis. The HRE is the first company from the <a href="/wiki/DAX" title="DAX">DAX</a> that had to be rescued by the government in recent memory. <a class="external text" href="http://www.handelsblatt.com/unternehmen/banken-versicherungen/staat-kommt-hypo-real-estate-zu-hilfe;2050596" rel="nofollow">(Handelsblatt.com)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>'s stock market had its worst one-day plunge in almost a decade, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Paulo_Stock_Exchange" title="São Paulo Stock Exchange">São Paulo Stock Exchange</a> sank 9.36% to 46,028.06 points, its steepest drop since 1999. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/brazilMktRpt/idUSN2939422720080929" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a></li>
<li>Russian <a href="/wiki/Russian_Trading_System" title="Russian Trading System">RTS</a> falls 7,1%, <a href="/wiki/Moscow_Interbank_Currency_Exchange" title="Moscow Interbank Currency Exchange">MICEX</a> 5,5%, as investors sell off assets on emerging markets on concerns that the U.S. government's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Proposed_bailout_of_United_States_financial_system" title="Proposed bailout of United States financial system">bailout plan</a> will not be enough to stem the financial crisis caused by the <a href="/wiki/United_States_housing_bubble" title="United States housing bubble">U.S. housing bubble</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/news/story/russian-equities-fall-sharply-risk/story.aspx?guid=%7BF464F5BA%2DC896%2D492C%2DBAF6%2DA9B4128A2F35%7D&amp;dist=hplatest" rel="nofollow">(MarketWatch)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Citigroup" title="Citigroup">Citigroup</a> acquires the banking operations of <a href="/wiki/Wachovia" title="Wachovia">Wachovia</a>, the troubled <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Charlotte,_N.C." title="Charlotte, N.C.">Charlotte, N.C.</a>-based bank. Under the agreement, Citigroup will absorb up to $42 billion of losses on a $312 billion pool of loans, while the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FDIC" title="FDIC">U.S. Government</a> will take losses beyond that. <a class="external text" href="http://www.marketwatch.com/news/story/citigroup-acquire-wachovia-banking-operations/story.aspx?guid=%7B58CDF657%2DA276%2D4B0A%2D8729%2D80A9F9D552A0%7D&amp;siteid=bnbh" rel="nofollow">(MarketWatch)</a></li>
<li>The Government of <a href="/wiki/Iceland" title="Iceland">Iceland</a> takes control of the country's number three bank, the struggling <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Glitnir_Bank" title="Glitnir Bank">Glitnir Bank</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/rbssFinancialServicesAndRealEstateNews/idUSLT50368720080929" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://www.iht.com/articles/ap/2008/09/29/business/EU-Iceland-Glitnir.php" rel="nofollow">(International Herald Tribune)</a></li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Parliament_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Parliament of the United Kingdom">British Government</a> confirm that the <a href="/wiki/Mortgage_loan" title="Mortgage loan">mortgage</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Loans" title="Loans">loans</a> components of <a href="/wiki/Bradford_%26_Bingley" title="Bradford &amp; Bingley">Bradford &amp; Bingley</a> will be nationalised, whilst the company's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Savings" title="Savings">savings</a> operations will be sold to the Spanish banking group, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grupo_Santander" title="Grupo Santander">Grupo Santander</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/1/hi/business/7641193.stm" rel="nofollow">(<i>BBC News</i>)</a> The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Economic_crisis_of_2008" title="Economic crisis of 2008">financial crisis</a> around Europe deepened with the nationalization of <a href="/wiki/Fortis_(finance)" title="Fortis (finance)">Fortis</a> and a cash infusion from the <a href="/wiki/Benelux" title="Benelux">Benelux</a> states amounting to €11.2 billion.</li>
<li>Intervention is needed to support the US's <a href="/wiki/Wachovia" title="Wachovia">Wachovia</a>, Britain's <a href="/wiki/Bradford_%26_Bingley" title="Bradford &amp; Bingley">Bradford &amp; Bingley</a>, Iceland's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Glitnir_Bank" title="Glitnir Bank">Glitnir</a>, Germany's <a href="/wiki/Hypo_Real_Estate" title="Hypo Real Estate">Hypo Real Estate</a> and the Belgian-Dutch group <a href="/wiki/Fortis_(finance)" title="Fortis (finance)">Fortis</a>, following on from the <a href="/wiki/Subprime_mortgage_crisis" title="Subprime mortgage crisis">Subprime mortgage crisis</a>. (Sources as already listed)</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">Dow Jones Industrial Average</a> has the biggest intra-day decline in its history as it drops by 777 points. <a class="external text" href="http://www.ny1.com/content/features/86427/dow-jones-suffers-largest-point-drop-in-history/Default.aspx" rel="nofollow">(NY1)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2008_Tripoli_Lebanon_car_bombing" title="2008 Tripoli Lebanon car bombing">car bomb</a> explodes near a bus carrying <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lebanese_Army" title="Lebanese Army">Lebanese Army</a> troops to work in <a href="/wiki/Tripoli,_Lebanon" title="Tripoli, Lebanon">Tripoli, Lebanon</a>, which kills at least five people and injures 25. <a class="external text" href="http://www.foxnews.com/story/0,2933,429465,00.html" rel="nofollow">(AP via Fox News)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Flood" title="Flood">Floods</a> caused by <a href="/wiki/Typhoon_Hagupit_(2008)" title="Typhoon Hagupit (2008)">Typhoon Hagupit</a> cause at least 41 deaths in northern <a href="/wiki/Vietnam" title="Vietnam">Vietnam</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news.com.au/story/0,10117,24418950-401,00.html" rel="nofollow">(News Limited)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a>’s official <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kronofogden" title="Kronofogden">debt collection agency</a> is suffering from severe economic problems after having over-spent and over-borrowed and may be forced to cut staff to stop the bleeding. <a class="external text" href="http://www.thelocal.se/14630/20080929/" rel="nofollow">(The Local)</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil">Brazil</a>'s government is named as the worst illegal logger of the <a href="/wiki/Amazon_rainforest" title="Amazon rainforest">Amazon rainforest</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/americas/7643346.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<tr>
<td style="text-align:left;font-size:11pt; font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px; width:100%"><span class="summary"><span style="display:none;">Current events of</span> September 30, 2008<span style="display:none"> (<span class="bday dtstart published updated">2008-09-30</span>)</span> (Tuesday)</span></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_30&amp;action=edit&amp;editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions">edit</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_30&amp;action=history">history</a></small></td>
<td style="text-align:right;font-weight:bold; padding:5px; margin-left:0px"><small class="editlink noprint"><a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2008_September_30&amp;action=watch">watch</a></small></td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td class="description">
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/2008_Chinese_milk_scandal" title="2008 Chinese milk scandal">2008 Chinese milk scandal</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">Dutch</a> food giant <a href="/wiki/Unilever" title="Unilever">Unilever</a> began recalling <a href="/wiki/Lipton" title="Lipton">Lipton</a>-brand milk tea powder in <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong" title="Hong Kong">Hong Kong</a> and <a href="/wiki/Macau" title="Macau">Macau</a> after they were found to contain traces of melamine. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbsnews.com/stories/2008/09/30/world/main4489172.shtml" rel="nofollow">(CBS News)</a></li>
<li>Chinese police report having arrested 22 people on Monday over melamine tainted milk products. <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/asia-pacific/7643391.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Shares of major Irish banks rise sharply following the announcement of a <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland" title="Republic of Ireland">State</a> guarantee of all deposits in <a href="/wiki/Allied_Irish_Banks" title="Allied Irish Banks">Allied Irish Banks</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_Ireland" title="Bank of Ireland">Bank of Ireland</a>, <a href="/wiki/Anglo_Irish_Bank" title="Anglo Irish Bank">Anglo Irish Bank</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Irish_Life_%26_Permanent" title="Irish Life &amp; Permanent">Irish Life &amp; Permanent</a>, <a href="/wiki/Irish_Nationwide_Building_Society" title="Irish Nationwide Building Society">Irish Nationwide Building Society</a> and <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Educational_Building_Society" title="Educational Building Society">EBS</a>, worth an estimated €400 billion. The guarantee includes Bank of Ireland branches in <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a> while the coverage of AIB's subsidiary, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/First_Trust" title="First Trust">First Trust</a> is still under discussion. Deposits in foreign-owned banks remain guaranteed to €100,000. <a class="external text" href="http://www.rte.ie/news/2008/0930/economy.html" rel="nofollow">(RTÉ News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/uk_news/northern_ireland/7644798.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li>147 people are dead after a <a href="/wiki/2008_Jodhpur_stampede" title="2008 Jodhpur stampede">human stampede</a> at the Chamunda <a href="/wiki/Hindu_temple" title="Hindu temple">Hindu temple</a> near <a href="/wiki/Jodhpur" title="Jodhpur">Jodhpur</a> in <a href="/wiki/India" title="India">India</a>. <a class="external text" href="http://www.reuters.com/article/topNews/idUSTRE48T0D720080930" rel="nofollow">(Reuters)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://edition.cnn.com/2008/WORLD/asiapcf/09/29/india.stampede/index.html?eref=rss_latest" rel="nofollow">(CNN)</a>, <a class="external text" href="http://www.canberratimes.com.au/news/local/news/general/indian-temple-stampede-death-toll-climbs/1321449.aspx?src=rss" rel="nofollow">(AFP via <i>The Canberra Times</i>)</a></li>
<li>At least 35 people die when a bus collides with a milk tanker and catches fire in central <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a>, police say. <a class="external text" href="http://www.news24.com/News24/World/Home/0,6130,2-10,00.html" rel="nofollow">(News 24)</a></li>
<li>30 suspected mobsters arrested around <a href="/wiki/Naples" title="Naples">Naples</a> in "war against the <a href="/wiki/Camorra" title="Camorra">Camorra</a>". <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/europe/7644290.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Piracy_in_Somalia" title="Piracy in Somalia">Piracy in Somalia</a>:
<ul>
<li>Pirates deny reports of three of their own killed in a shoot-out aboard the Ukrainian ship (<a href="/wiki/MV_Faina" title="MV Faina">MV Faina</a>) off the African coast. <a class="external text" href="http://www.cbc.ca/world/story/2008/09/30/somalia-pirates.html" rel="nofollow">(CBC News)</a> <a class="external text" href="http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/africa/7643561.stm" rel="nofollow">(BBC News)</a></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Dow_Jones_Industrial_Average" title="Dow Jones Industrial Average">Dow Jones Industrial Average</a> goes up almost 500 points, following its largest one day point drop in history yesterday.<a class="external text" href="http://biz.yahoo.com/ap/080930/wall_street.html" rel="nofollow">(Yahoo Finance)</a></li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
</table>
</td>

<tr style="background-color: #f5faff;">
<td>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="September"><a href="/wiki/Deaths_in_September_2008" title="Deaths in September 2008">September</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/September_2008/Sidebar&amp;action=edit&amp;section=T-1" title="Portal:Current events/September 2008/Sidebar">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_26" title="September 26">26</a>: <a href="/wiki/Paul_Newman" title="Paul Newman">Paul Newman</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_25" title="September 25">25</a>: <a href="/wiki/Ralph_Sazio" title="Ralph Sazio">Ralph Sazio</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_25" title="September 25">25</a>: <a href="/wiki/Glenn_Andrews" title="Glenn Andrews">Glenn Andrews</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_24" title="September 24">24</a>: <a href="/wiki/Sonja_Savi%C4%87" title="Sonja Savić">Sonja Savić</a></li>
